dataclasses import dataclassfrom datetime import datetime, timedelta, timefrom typing import List, Optional, Dict, Callablefrom enum import Enumimport asyncioimport logginglogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)class RecurrenceType(Enum):    ONCE = "once"    DAILY = "daily"    WEEKLY = "weekly"    MONTHLY = "monthly"    SUNRISE = "sunrise"  # יחסית לזריחה    SUNSET = "sunset"    # יחסית לשקיעה    GOLDEN_HOUR = "golden_hour"@dataclassclass ScheduledMission:    id: str    name: str    mission_type: str    schedule_time: datetime    recurrence: RecurrenceType    drone_id: str    parameters: Dict    enabled: bool = True    last_run: Optional[datetime] = None    next_run: Optional[datetime] = None    max_retries: int = 3    retry_count: int = 0        def calculate_next_run(self, sunrise_time: time = None, sunset_time: time = None):        """חשב את הריצה הבאה"""        if self.recurrence == RecurrenceType.ONCE:            return None if self.last_run else self.schedule_time                base = self.last_run or self.schedule_time                if self.recurrence == RecurrenceType.DAILY:            return base + timedelta(days=1)        elif self.recurrence == RecurrenceType.WEEKLY:            return base + timedelta(weeks=1)        elif self.recurrence == RecurrenceType.MONTHLY:            # פשוט — חודש + 30 יום            return base + timedelta(days=30)        elif self.recurrence == RecurrenceType.SUNRISE and sunrise_time:            tomorrow = base.date() + timedelta(days=1)            return datetime.combine(tomorrow, sunrise_time)        elif self.recurrence == RecurrenceType.SUNSET and sunset_time:            tomorrow = base.date() + timedelta(days=1)            return datetime.combine(tomorrow, sunset_time)                return Noneclass MissionScheduler:    """מתזמן משימות חכם"""        def __init__(self, weather_service, sun_service):        self.weather = weather_service        self.sun = sun_service        self.missions: Dict[str, ScheduledMission] = {}        self._running = False        self._task = None        self._callbacks: List[Callable] = []        def add_mission(self, mission: ScheduledMission):        """הוסף משימה מתוזמנת"""        # חשב next_run ראשוני        sunrise, sunset = self._get_sun_times(mission.schedule_time)        mission.next_run = mission.calculate_next_run(sunrise, sunset)                self.missions[mission.id] = mission        logger.info(f"משימה מתוזמנת נוספה: {mission.name} ב-{mission.next_run}")        def remove_mission(self, mission_id: str):        """הסר משימה"""        if mission_id in self.missions:            del self.missions[mission_id]        async def start(self):        """התחל מתזמן"""        self._running = True        self._task = asyncio.create_task(self._scheduler_loop())        logger.info("מתזמן התחיל")        async def stop(self):        """עצור מתזמן"""        self._running = False        if self._task:            self._task.cancel()            try:                await self._task            except asyncio.CancelledError:                pass        async def _scheduler_loop(self):        """לולאת מתזמן ראשית"""        while self._running:            now = datetime.now()                        for mission in self.missions.values():                if not mission.enabled:                    continue                                if mission.next_run and mission.next_run <= now:                    # בדוק תנאים                    if await self._check_conditions(mission):                        await self._execute_mission(mission)                    else:                        logger.warning(f"תנאים לא מתאימים ל-{mission.name}, נדחה")                        mission.next_run = now + timedelta(hours=1)                        await asyncio.sleep(60)  # בדוק כל דקה        async def _check_conditions(self, mission: ScheduledMission) -> bool:        """בדוק אם תנאי מזג אוויר ובטיחות מתאימים"""        # בדוק מזג אוויר        wx = await self.weather.get_forecast(            location=mission.parameters.get('location'),            time=mission.next_run        )                limits = mission.parameters.get('weather_limits', {})        max_wind = limits.get('max_wind_ms', 10)        no_rain = limits.get('no_precipitation', True)        min_visibility = limits.get('min_visibility_km', 5)                if wx.wind_speed_ms > max_wind:            logger.info(f"רוח חזקה מדי: {wx.wind_speed_ms} מ'/ש'")            return False                if no_rain and wx.precipitation_probability > 0.3:            logger.info(f"סיכוי גשם: {wx.precipitation_probability*100}%")            return False                if wx.visibility_km < min_visibility:            logger.info(f"ראות נמוכה: {wx.visibility_km} ק\"מ")            return False                # בדוק מרחב אווירי        # TODO: אינטגרציה עם OpenAIP                # בדוק סוללה/תחזוקה        # TODO: בדיקת תחזוקה דרון                return True        async def _execute_mission(self, mission: ScheduledMission):        """בצע משימה מתוזמנת"""        logger.info(f"מבצע משימה מתוזמנת: {mission.name}")                try:            # קרא callbacks            for callback in self._callbacks:                await callback('mission_starting', mission)                        # בצע            # TODO: אינטגרציה עם MissionController                        mission.last_run = datetime.now()            mission.retry_count = 0                        # חשב next_run הבא            sunrise, sunset = self._get_sun_times(mission.last_run)            mission.next_run = mission.calculate_next_run(sunrise, sunset)                        for callback in self._callbacks:                await callback('mission_completed', mission)                        except Exception as e:            logger.error(f"משימה נכשלה: {e}")            mission.retry_count += 1                        if mission.retry_count >= mission.max_retries:                logger.error(f"מקסימום ניסיונות חזרו עבור {mission.name}")                mission.enabled = False            else:                # נסה שוב בעוד שעה                mission.next_run = datetime.now() + timedelta(hours=1)        def _get_sun_times(self, date: datetime) -> tuple:        """קבל זמני זריחה/שקיעה"""        # TODO: חישוב אסטרונומי או API        return time(6, 0), time(18, 0)        def on_event(self, callback: Callable):        """רשם callback לאירועים"""        self._callbacks.append(callback)        def get_upcoming(self, hours: int = 24) -> List[ScheduledMission]:        """קבל משימות קרובות"""        now = datetime.now()        cutoff = now + timedelta(hours=hours)                upcoming = []        for mission in self.missions.values():            if mission.enabled and mission.next_run:                if now <= mission.next_run <= cutoff:                    upcoming.append(mission)                return sorted(upcoming, key=lambda m: m.next_run)31. מערכת סימולציה מתקדמת# skycore/simulator/advanced.pyimport numpy as npfrom dataclasses import dataclassfrom typing import List, Tuple, Optionalimport asyncio@dataclassclass SimulatedEnvironment:    """סביבה מדומה"""    wind_velocity: Tuple[float, float, float]  # m/s (x, y, z)    wind_gusts: float  # עוצמת משבים    temperature_c: float    pressure_hpa: float    magnetic_declination: float  # מעלות        # מכשולים    obstacles: List[dict] = None  # מבנים, עצים, כבלים@dataclassclass SimulatedDroneState:    """מצב רחפן מדומה"""    position: np.ndarray  # [x, y, z] מטרים    velocity: np.ndarray  # [vx, vy, vz] מ'/ש'    attitude: np.ndarray  # [roll, pitch, yaw] רדיאנים    angular_velocity: np.ndarray  # [p, q, r] רדיאן/ש        # מנועים    motor_rpms: np.ndarray  # [m1, m2, m3, m4]    motor_temperatures: np.ndarray        # סוללה    battery_voltage: float    battery_current: float    battery_percent: float        # חיישנים    gps_position: Optional[Tuple[float, float, float]]    gps_accuracy: float  # HDOP    barometer_altitude: float    imu_acceleration: np.ndarray    imu_gyroscope: np.ndarrayclass PhysicsEngine:    """מנוע פיזיקה לסימולציה"""        # קבועים פיזיקליים    GRAVITY = 9.81  # m/s²    AIR_DENSITY = 1.225  # kg/m³ at sea level        def __init__(self, drone_mass_kg: float = 0.9):        self.mass = drone_mass_kg        self.drag_coefficient = 0.47  # כדור approximate        self.cross_sectional_area = 0.05  # m²                # מומנטים התמד (Inertia) — approximate for quadcopter        self.Ixx = 0.01  # kg·m²        self.Iyy = 0.01        self.Izz = 0.02        def calculate_forces(        self,        state: SimulatedDroneState,        motor_thrusts: np.ndarray,        environment: SimulatedEnvironment    ) -> Tuple[np.ndarray, np.ndarray]:        """        חשב כוחות ומומנטים                Returns:            forces: [Fx, Fy, Fz] ב-Newtons            moments: [Mx, My, Mz] ב-N·m        """        # כוחות מנועים (למעלה — שלילי z)        total_thrust = np.sum(motor_thrusts)        thrust_vector = np.array([0, 0, -total_thrust])                # כוח משקל        gravity = np.array([0, 0, self.mass * self.GRAVITY])                # כוח רוח        wind_force = self._calculate_wind_force(            state.velocity,            environment.wind_velocity,            environment.wind_gusts        )                # כוח גרר (drag)        drag = -0.5 * self.AIR_DENSITY * self.cross_sectional_area * self.drag_coefficient * np.linalg.norm(state.velocity) * state.velocity                # סך הכוחות        forces = thrust_vector + gravity + wind_force + drag                # מומנטים (torques) — פשוט        # TODO: מודל מנועים מפורט יותר        moments = np.array([            (motor_thrusts[3] - motor_thrusts[1]) * 0.1,  # roll            (motor_thrusts[2] - motor_thrusts[0]) * 0.1,  # pitch            0.0  # yaw — TODO        ])                return forces, moments        def _calculate_wind_force(        self,        velocity: np.ndarray,        wind_velocity: np.ndarray,        gust_factor: float    ) -> np.ndarray:        """חשב כוח רוח"""        relative_velocity = wind_velocity - velocity                # הוסף משבים אקראיים        gust = np.random.normal(0, gust_factor, 3)                # כוח פרופורציונלי לריבוע המהירות        wind_speed = np.linalg.norm(relative_velocity + gust)        direction = (relative_velocity + gust) / (wind_speed + 0.001)                force_magnitude = 0.5 * self.AIR_DENSITY * self.cross_sectional_area * wind_speed**2                return force_magnitude * direction        def integrate(        self,        state: SimulatedDroneState,        forces: np.ndarray,        moments: np.ndarray,        dt: float    ) -> SimulatedDroneState:        """        אינטגרציה — Euler פשוט (ניתן לשדרג ל-RK4)        """        # תאוצה קוויתית        acceleration = forces / self.mass                # עדכן מהירות        new_velocity = state.velocity + acceleration * dt                # עדכן מיקום        new_position = state.position + state.velocity * dt + 0.5 * acceleration * dt**2                # תאוצה זוויתית        # τ = I·α  =>  α = I⁻¹·τ        angular_acceleration = np.array([            moments[0] / self.Ixx,            moments[1] / self.Iyy,            moments[2] / self.Izz        ])                # עדכן מהירות זוויתית        new_angular_velocity = state.angular_velocity + angular_acceleration * dt                # עדכן זוויות (פשוט — לא מטפל ב-singularities)        new_attitude = state.attitude + state.angular_velocity * dt                # עטוף yaw ל-[-π, π]        new_attitude[2] = (new_attitude[2] + np.pi) % (2 * np.pi) - np.pi                # עדכן סוללה        power = np.sum(state.motor_rpms * 0.01)  # פשוט        new_voltage = state.battery_voltage - power * dt * 0.001        new_percent = max(0, (new_voltage - 14.0) / (16.8 - 14.0) * 100)                return SimulatedDroneState(            position=new_position,            velocity=new_velocity,            attitude=new_attitude,            angular_velocity=new_angular_velocity,            motor_rpms=state.motor_rpms,            motor_temperatures=state.motor_temperatures + 0.1 * dt,            battery_voltage=new_voltage,            battery_current=power / new_voltage if new_voltage > 0 else 0,            battery_percent=new_percent,            gps_position=self._add_gps_noise(new_position),            gps_accuracy=1.0 + np.random.exponential(0.5),            barometer_altitude=new_position[2] + np.random.normal(0, 0.5),            imu_acceleration=acceleration + np.random.normal(0, 0.01, 3),            imu_gyroscope=new_angular_velocity + np.random.normal(0, 0.001, 3)        )        def _add_gps_noise(self, position: np.ndarray) -> Tuple[float, float, float]:        """הוסף רעש GPS ריאליסטי"""        # המרה פשוטה מ-local ל-GPS — לא מדויק!        noise = np.random.normal(0, 2.0, 2)  # 2 מטרים רעש        return (            32.0853 + position[0] * 0.00001 + noise[0] * 0.00001,            34.7818 + position[1] * 0.00001 + noise[1] * 0.00001,            position[2] + np.random.normal(0, 1.0)        )class AdvancedSimulator:    """סימולטור מתקדם עם פיזיקה ריאליסטית"""        def __init__(self, drone_config: dict):        self.physics = PhysicsEngine(            drone_mass_kg=drone_config.get('mass_kg', 0.9)        )        self.state: Optional[SimulatedDroneState] = None        self.environment = SimulatedEnvironment(            wind_velocity=(2.0, 1.0, 0.0),            wind_gusts=1.5,            temperature_c=25.0,            pressure_hpa=1013.25,            magnetic_declination=3.5        )        self._dt = 0.01  # 100 Hz physics        self._running = False        async def initialize(self, start_position: Tuple[float, float, float] = (0, 0, 0)):        """אתחל סימולטור"""        self.state = SimulatedDroneState(            position=np.array(start_position, dtype=float),            velocity=np.zeros(3),            attitude=np.zeros(3),            angular_velocity=np.zeros(3),            motor_rpms=np.array([0, 0, 0, 0], dtype=float),            motor_temperatures=np.array([25.0, 25.0, 25.0, 25.0]),            battery_voltage=16.8,            battery_current=0.0,            battery_percent=100.0,            gps_position=None,            gps_accuracy=99.0,            barometer_altitude=0.0,            imu_acceleration=np.zeros(3),            imu_gyroscope=np.zeros(3)        )        logger.info("סימולטור אתחול")        async def run_simulation(self):        """הרץ לולאת סימולציה"""        self._running = True                while self._running:            # קבל פקודות מנוע (מבקר)            motor_commands = await self._get_motor_commands()                        # חשב כוחות            forces, moments = self.physics.calculate_forces(                self.state,                motor_commands,                self.environment            )                        # אינטגרציה            self.state = self.physics.integrate(                self.state,                forces,                moments,                self._dt            )                        # בדוק תקלות            if self.state.battery_percent <= 0:                logger.error("סוללה ריקה — סימולציה נעצרה")                self._running = False                        await asyncio.sleep(self._dt)        async def _get_motor_commands(self) -> np.ndarray:        """קבל פקודות מנוע — stub למבקר"""        # TODO: חיבור ל-flight controller מדומה        return np.array([1.0, 1.0, 1.0, 1.0]) * self.mass * self.physics.GRAVITY / 4        def set_wind(self, velocity: Tuple[float, float, float], gusts: float = 0):        """שנה תנאי רוח"""        self.environment.wind_velocity = velocity        self.environment.wind_gusts = gusts        def add_obstacle(self, position: Tuple[float, float, float], radius: float):        """הוסף מכשול"""        if self.environment.obstacles is None:            self.environment.obstacles = []        self.environment.obstacles.append({            'position': position,            'radius': radius        })        def get_telemetry(self) -> dict:        """קבל טלמטריה נוכחית"""        if not self.state:            return {}                return {            'position': {                'x': float(self.state.position[0]),                'y': float(self.state.position[1]),                'z': float(self.state.position[2])            },            'velocity': {                'x': float(self.state.velocity[0]),                'y': float(self.state.velocity[1]),                'z': float(self.state.velocity[2])            },            'attitude': {                'roll': float(np.degrees(self.state.attitude[0])),                'pitch': float(np.degrees(self.state.attitude[1])),                'yaw': float(np.degrees(self.state.attitude[2]))            },            'battery': {                'percent': float(self.state.battery_percent),                'voltage': float(self.state.battery_voltage),                'current': float(self.state.battery_current)            },            'gps': {                'lat': self.state.gps_position[0] if self.state.gps_position else 0,                'lon': self.state.gps_position[1] if self.state.gps_position else 0,                'satellites': 12,                'hdop': float(self.state.gps_accuracy)            }        }32. מערכת בדיקות מקיפה# tests/test_integration.pyimport pytestimport asynciofrom datetime import datetimefrom skycore import 'skycore_flight_duration_seconds',    'משך טיסה',    buckets=[60, 300, 600, 1800, 3600])BATTERY_LEVEL = Gauge(    'skycore_battery_percent',    'אחוז סוללה',    ['drone_id'])TELEMETRY_LATENCY = 'skycore_active_connections',    'חיבורים פעילים')class MetricsExporter:    """מייצא מדדים ל-Prometheus"""        def __init__(self, port: int = 9090):        self.port = port        self._running = datetime import datetimeimport logginglogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)class CloudSync:    """סנכרון אוטומטי לענן (S3-compatible)"""        def __init__(        self,        endpoint_url: str,        access_key: str,        secret_key: str,        bucket: str,        region: str = "us-east-1"    ):        self.s3 = boto3.client(            's3',            endpoint_url=endpoint_url,            aws_access_key_id=access_key,            aws_secret_access_key=secret_key,            region_name=region        )        self.bucket = bucket        async def upload_flight_data(        self,        flight_id: str,        local_dir: Path,        include_video: bool = True,        include_logs: bool = True,        include_photos: bool = True    ) -> dict:        """העלה נתוני טיסה לענן"""        uploaded = []        failed = []                # צור מטא-דאטה        metadata = {            'flight_id': flight_id,            'uploaded_at': datetime.now().isoformat(),            'files': []        }                # אסוף קבצים        files_to_upload = []                if include_logs:            files_to_upload.extend(local_dir.glob("*.csv"))            files_to_upload.extend(local_dir.glob("*.json"))                if include_video:            files_to_upload.extend(local_dir.glob("*.mp4"))                if include_photos:            files_to_upload.extend(local_dir.glob("*.jpg"))            files_to_upload.extend(local_dir.glob("*.dng"))                # העלה        for file_path in files_to_upload:            try:                key = f"flights/{flight_id}/{file_path.name}"                                # בדוק אם כבר קיים (hash)                local_hash = self._file_hash(file_path)                                try:                    head = self.s3.head_object(Bucket=self.bucket, Key=key)                    remote_hash = head['Metadata'].get('sha256', '')                                        if local_hash == remote_hash:                        logger.info(f"קובץ זהה כבר בענן: {file_path.name}")                        continue                except ClientError:                    pass  # לא קיים                                # העלה                self.s3.upload_file(                    str(file_path),                    self.bucket,                    key,                    ExtraArgs={                        'Metadata': {'sha256': local_hash},                        'ContentType': self._guess_mime(file_path.suffix)                    }                )                                uploaded.append({                    'filename': file_path.name,                    'size': file_path.stat().st_size,                    'hash': local_hash,                    's3_key': key                })                                logger.info(f"הועלה: {file_path.name}")                            except Exception as e:                logger.error(f"שגיאת העלאה {file_path.name}: {e}")                failed.append({'filename': file_path.name, 'error': str(e)})                # שמור מטא-דאטה        metadata['files'] = uploaded        metadata['failed'] = failed                self.s3.put_object(            Bucket=self.bucket,            Key=f"flights/{flight_id}/metadata.json",            Body=json.dumps(metadata, indent=2),            ContentType='application/json'        )                return {            'flight_id': flight_id,            'uploaded_count': len(uploaded),            'failed_count': len(failed),            'total_size': sum(f['size'] for f in uploaded)        }        async def download_flight_data(        self,        flight_id: str,        local_dir: Path,        file_types: Optional[List[str]] = None    ) -> List[Path]:        """הורד נתוני טיסה מהענן"""        downloaded = []                # קבל רשימת קבצים        prefix = f"flights/{flight_id}/"        response = self.s3.list_objects_v2(            Bucket=self.bucket,            Prefix=prefix        )                for obj in response.get('Contents', []):            key = obj['Key']            filename = Path(key).name                        # סנן לפי סוג            if file_types:                suffix = Path(filename).suffix.lower()                if suffix not in file_types:                    continue                        # הורד            local_path = local_dir / filename            local_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)                        self.s3.download_file(self.bucket, key, str(local_path))            downloaded.append(local_path)                        logger.info(f"הורד: {filename}")                return downloaded        async def list_flights(        self,        start_date: Optional[datetime] = None,        end_date: Optional[datetime] = None    ) -> List[dict]:        """רשום טיסות שבענן"""        flights = []                # קבל metadata files        response = self.s3.list_objects_v2(            Bucket=self.bucket,            Prefix='flights/',            Delimiter='/'        )                for prefix in response.get('CommonPrefixes', []):            flight_id = prefix['Prefix'].split('/')[-2]                        try:                meta_obj = self.s3.get_object(                    Bucket=self.bucket,                    Key=f"{prefix['Prefix']}metadata.json"                )                metadata = json.loads(meta_obj['Body'].read())                                # סנן לפי תאריך                flight_date = datetime.fromisoformat(metadata.get('uploaded_at', ''))                                if start_date and flight_date < start_date:                    continue                if end_date and flight_date > end_date:                    continue                                flights.append({                    'flight_id': flight_id,                    'date': flight_date.isoformat(),                    'files_count': len(metadata.get('files', [])),                    'total_size': sum(f.get('size', 0) for f in metadata.get('files', []))                })                            except ClientError:                continue                return sorted(flights, key=lambda x: x['date'], reverse=True)        def _file_hash(self, path: Path) -> str:        """חשב SHA-256 של קובץ"""        h = hashlib.sha256()        with open(path, 'rb') as f:            for chunk in iter(lambda: f.read(8192), b''):                h.update(chunk)        return h.hexdigest()        def _guess_mime(self, suffix: str) -> str:        """נחש MIME type"""        types = {            '.mp4': 'video/mp4',            '.jpg': 'image/jpeg',            '.dng': 'image/x-adobe-dng',            '.csv': 'text/csv',            '.json': 'application/json',            '.log': 'text/plain'        }        return types.get(suffix.lower(), 'application/octet-stream')36. מערכת דוחות אוטומטית EmailReporter:    """שלח דוחות באימייל"""        def __init__(self, smtp_host: str, smtp_port: int, username: str, password: str):        self.smtp_host = smtp_host        self.smtp_port = smtp_port skycore/hil/tester.pyimport asynciofrom dataclasses import dataclassfrom typing import Dict, List, Optional, Callableimport serialimport struct@dataclassclass HILConfig:    """תצורת בדיקת חומרה"""    serial_port: str  # COM3, /dev/ttyUSB0    baudrate: int = 921600    protocol: str = "mavlink"  # או "dji", "custom"    test_duration_sec: float = 60.0class HardwareInLoopTester:    """בודק חומרה אמיתית בסימולציה"""        def __init__(self, config: HILConfig):        self.config = config        self.serial: Optional[serial.Serial] = None        self._running = False        self._tests: List[Callable] = []        self._results: Dict[str, dict] = {}        async def connect(self) -> bool:        """חבר לבקר טיסה אמיתי"""        try:            self.serial = serial.Serial(                port=self.config.serial_port,                baudrate=self.config.baudrate,                timeout=1            )            logger.info(f"מחובר ל-{self.config.serial_port}")            return True        except Exception as e:            logger.error(f"שגיאת חיבור: {e}")            return False        async def run_test_suite(self) -> Dict[str, bool]:        """הרץ סדרת בדיקות"""        if not self.serial:            raise RuntimeError("לא מחובר לחומרה")                self._running = True                for test in self._tests:            test_name = test.__name__            logger.info(f"מבצע בדיקה: {test_name}")                        try:                result = await test()                self._results[test_name] = {                    'passed': result,                    'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat()                }            except Exception as e:                logger.error(f"בדיקה נכשלה: {e}")                self._results[test_name] = {                    'passed': False,                    'error': str(e)                }                self._running = False        return {k: v['passed'] for k, v in self._results.items()}        async def test_motor_response(self) -> bool:        """בדוק תגובת מנועים"""        # שלח פקודות מנוע עולות        for throttle in [0, 25, 50, 75, 100]:            cmd = self._pack_motor_command([throttle] * 4)            self.serial.write(cmd)                        # קבל משוב            await asyncio.sleep(0.1)            feedback = self.serial.read(64)                        # בדוק תקינות            rpm = self._parse_rpm(feedback)            expected_rpm = throttle * 100  # פשוט                        if abs(rpm[0] - expected_rpm) > 500:                logger.warning(f"מנוע 1 לא תקין: {rpm[0]} RPM, צפוי {expected_rpm}")                return False                return True        async def test_imu_calibration(self) -> bool:        """בדוק כיול IMU"""        # בקש סטטוס כיול        self.serial.write(self._pack_imu_status_request())                await asyncio.sleep(0.5)        response = self.serial.read(128)                status = self._parse_imu_status(response)                checks = [            status['accel_calibrated'],            status['gyro_calibrated'],            status['mag_calibrated']        ]                return all(checks)        async def test_gps_lock(self) -> bool:        """בדוק נעילת GPS"""        timeout = 300  # 5 דקות מקסימום                for _ in range(timeout):            self.serial.write(self._pack_gps_request())            await asyncio.sleep(1)                        response = self.serial.read(256)            gps = self._parse_gps(response)                        if gps['satellites'] >= 8 and gps['hdop'] < 2.0:                logger.info(f"GPS נעול: {gps['satellites']} לוויינים")                return True                logger.error("GPS לא נעול בזמן")        return False        async def test_rc_link(self) -> bool:        """בדוק קישור שלט"""        # בדוק RSSI        self.serial.write(self._pack_rc_status_request())                await asyncio.sleep(0.2)        response = self.serial.read(64)                rc = self._parse_rc_status(response)                return rc['rssi'] > -80  # dBm        async def test_battery_monitoring(self) -> bool:        """בדוק ניטור סוללה"""        # בדוק מתח        self.serial.write(self._pack_battery_request())                await asyncio.sleep(0.1)        response = self.serial.read(64)                battery = self._parse_battery(response)                checks = [            10.0 < battery['voltage'] < 17.0,  # 3S-4S            battery['current'] >= 0,            0 < battery['percent'] <= 100        ]                return all(checks)        def add_test(self, test_func: Callable):        """הוסף בדיקה מותאמת"""        self._tests.append(test_func)        def _pack_motor_command(self, throttles: List[int]) -> bytes:        """ארוז פקודת מנוע"""        # MAVLink או פרוטוקול מותאם        return struct.pack('<4H', *throttles)  # פשוט        def _parse_rpm(self, data: bytes) -> List[int]:        """פארס RPM"""        if len(data) < 8:            return [0, 0, 0, 0]        return list(struct.unpack('<4H', data[:8]))        def _pack_imu_status_request(self) -> bytes:        return b'\x01\x02'  # stub        def _parse_imu_status(self, data: bytes) -> dict:        return {'accel_calibrated': True, 'gyro_calibrated': True, 'mag_calibrated': True}        def _pack_gps_request(self) -> bytes:        return b'\x01\x03'  # stub        def _parse_gps(self, data: bytes) -> dict:        return {'satellites': 12, 'hdop': 1.2, 'lat': 32.0, 'lon': 34.0}        def _pack_rc_status_request(self) -> bytes:        return b'\x01\x04'  # stub        def _parse_rc_status(self, data: bytes) -> dict:        return {'rssi': -65, 'channels': [1500] * 16}        def _pack_battery_request(self) -> bytes:        return b'\x01\x05'  # stub        def _parse_battery(self, data: bytes) -> dict:        return {'voltage': 16.4, 'current': 5.2, 'percent': 85}38. טבלת תאימות סופית ומעודכנת (מאי 2026)דגםסטטוסSDKטווח datetime import datetimefrom typing import Dict, List, Optional, Tuplefrom enum import Enumimport hashlibimport loggingimport requestslogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)class FirmwareStatus(Enum):    CURRENT = "current"           # גרסה נוכחית — עדכנית    UPDATE_AVAILABLE = "available"  # יש עדכון    MANDATORY = "mandatory"       # עדכון חובה    BETA = "beta"                 # גרסת בטא    UNSUPPORTED = "unsupported"   # לא נתמך יותר@dataclassclass FirmwareVersion:    version: str                    # לדוג' "01.00.0500"    release_date: datetime    changelog: str    download_url: Optional[str]    hash_sha256: str    size_mb: float    is_mandatory: bool = False    is_beta: bool = False        def compare_to(self, other: 'FirmwareVersion') -> int:        """השווה גרסאות. מחזיר: -1 (ישן), 0 (זהה), 1 (חדש)"""        v1 = self._parse_version(self.version)        v2 = self._parse_version(other.version)                for a, b in zip(v1, v2):            if a < b: return -1            if a > b: return 1                return 0        def _parse_version(self, v: str) -> Tuple[int, ...]:        """פארס מחרוזת גרסה למספרים"""        return tuple(int(x) for x in v.split('.'))class FirmwareManager:    """מנהל קושחה — רק עדכונים רשמיים מ-DJI"""        DJI_FIRMWARE_URL = "https://www.dji.com/api/firmware"  # stub        def __init__(self):        self._installed: Dict[str, FirmwareVersion] = {}  # drone_id -> version        self._available: Dict[str, List[FirmwareVersion]] = {}  # model -> versions        self._cache_dir = "./cache/firmware"        async def check_updates(self, drone_id: str, model: str, current_version: str) -> FirmwareStatus:        """בדוק אם יש עדכון זמין"""        current = FirmwareVersion(            version=current_version,            release_date=datetime.now(),  # לא ידוע            changelog="",            hash_sha256="",            size_mb=0        )                # קבל רשימת גרסאות זמינות        available = await self._fetch_available_versions(model)                if not available:            return FirmwareStatus.CURRENT                latest = available[0]  # ממוין — החדש ביותר ראשון                comparison = current.compare_to(latest)                if comparison >= 0:            return FirmwareStatus.CURRENT                if latest.is_mandatory:            return FirmwareStatus.MANDATORY                if latest.is_beta:            return FirmwareStatus.BETA                return FirmwareStatus.UPDATE_AVAILABLE        async def download_firmware(        self,        version: FirmwareVersion,        progress_callback: Optional[callable] = None    ) -> Optional[str]:        """הורד קושחה רשמית"""        if not version.download_url:            logger.error("אין URL להורדה")            return None                local_path = f"{self._cache_dir}/{version.hash_sha256}.zip"                # בדוק אם כבר קיים        if self._verify_file(local_path, version.hash_sha256):            logger.info("קובץ כבר קיים ותקין")            return local_path                # הורד        logger.info(f"מוריד קושחה {version.version}...")                response = requests.get(version.download_url, stream=True)        total_size = int(response.headers.get('content-length', 0))                downloaded = 0        with open(local_path, 'wb') as f:            for chunk in response.iter_content(chunk_size=8192):                f.write(chunk)                downloaded += len(chunk)                                if progress_callback:                    progress = downloaded / total_size * 100                    await progress_callback(progress)                # אמת hash        if not self._verify_file(local_path, version.hash_sha256):            logger.error("Hash לא תואם! קובץ פגום.")            return None                logger.info(f"הורדה הושלמה: {local_path}")        return local_path        def _verify_file(self, path: str, expected_hash: str) -> bool:        """אמת שלמות קובץ"""        try:            h = hashlib.sha256()            with open(path, 'rb') as f:                for chunk in iter(lambda: f.read(8192), b''):                    h.update(chunk)            return h.hexdigest().lower() == expected_hash.lower()        except FileNotFoundError:            return False        async def _fetch_available_versions(self, model: str) -> List[FirmwareVersion]:        """קבל רשימת גרסאות מ-DJI"""        # TODO: אינטגרציה אמיתית עם API של DJI        # כרגע — stub                return [            FirmwareVersion(                version="01.00.0600",                release_date=datetime(2026, 4, 15),                changelog="שיפורי יציבות, תיקוני באגים",                download_url=None,  # דורש אימות                hash_sha256="abcd1234...",                size_mb=245.5,                is_mandatory=False            ),            FirmwareVersion( False40. מערכת כיול חיישנים אוטומטית# skycore/calibration/sensors.pyimport numpy as npfrom dataclasses import dataclassfrom typing import List, Tuple, Optionalfrom enum import Enumimport asyncioimport logginglogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)class CalibrationStatus(Enum):    IDLE = "idle"    IN_PROGRESS = "in_progress"    COMPLETED = "completed"    FAILED = "failed"    ABORTED = "aborted"@dataclassclass IMUCalibrationData:    accel_offset: np.ndarray      # [ax, ay, az]    accel_scale: np.ndarray       # [sx, sy, sz]    gyro_offset: np.ndarray       # [gx, gy, gz]    mag_hard_iron: np.ndarray     # [hx, hy, hz]    mag_soft_iron: np.ndarray     # 3x3 matrix        temperature_compensation: Optional[dict] = Noneclass SensorCalibrator:    """מכייל חיישנים אוטומטית"""        # קבועים    ACCEL_POSITIONS = 6    # 6 צדדים    GYRO_SAMPLES = 1000    # דגימות לכיול ג'ירו    MAG_ROTATIONS = 3      # צירים לסיבוב        def __init__(self, drone):        self.drone = drone        self.status = CalibrationStatus.IDLE        self.progress = 0.0  # 0-100        async def calibrate_imu_full(self) -> bool:        """כיול IMU מלא — 6 צדדים"""        self.status = CalibrationStatus.IN_PROGRESS        self.progress = 0                try:            # 1. כיול תאוצה            accel_data = await self._calibrate_accelerometer()            self.progress = 33                        # 2. כיול ג'ירו            gyro_data = await self._calibrate_gyroscope()            self.progress = 66                        # 3. כיול מצפן            mag_data = await  accel_scale=accel_data['scale'],                gyro_offset=gyro_data['offset'],                mag_hard_iron=mag_data['hard_iron'],                mag_soft_iron=mag_data['soft_iron']            )                        await self._save_calibration(calibration)                        self.status = CalibrationStatus.COMPLETED            logger.info("כיול IMU הושלם")            return True                    except Exception as e:            self.status = CalibrationStatus.FAILED            logger.error(f"כיול נכשל: {e}")            return False        async def _calibrate_accelerometer(self) -> dict:        """כיול תאוצה — שיטת 6 צדדים"""        logger.info("מתחיל כיול תאוצה...")                measurements = []                # הוראות למשתמש (או אוטומציה עם gimbal)        positions = [            "Z+ למעלה (רגיל)",            "Z- למטה (הפוך)",            "Y+ למעלה",            "Y- למטה",            "X+ למעלה",            "X- למטה"        ]                for i, pos in enumerate(positions):            logger.info(f"מיקום {i+1}/{len(positions)}: {pos}")                        # המתן יציבות            await asyncio.sleep(2)                        # אסוף דגימות            samples = []            for _ in range(100):                accel = await self.drone.sensors.get_accelerometer()                samples.append(accel)                await asyncio.sleep(0.01)                        measurements.append(np.mean(samples, axis=0))            logger.info(f"  מדידה: {measurements[-1]}")                # חשב offset ו-scale        # שיטה: לפחות ריבועים        measurements = np.array(measurements)                # offset = ממוצע כל המדידות        offset = np.mean(measurements, axis=0)                # scale = התאמה ל-1g בכל ציר        expected = np.array([            [0, 0, 1],   # Z+            [0, 0, -1],  # Z-            [0, 1, 0],   # Y+            [0, -1, 0],  # Y-            [1, 0, 0],   # X+            [-1, 0, 0]   # X-        ]) * 9.81  # m/s²                # פתרון ל-scale (פשוט)        scale = np.ones(3)        for axis in range(3):            pos_idx = [4, 2, 0]  # X+, Y+, Z+            neg_idx = [5, 3, 1]  # X-, Y-, Z-                        pos_val = measurements[pos_idx[axis], axis] - offset[axis]            neg_val = measurements[neg_idx[axis], axis] - offset[axis]                        expected_range = expected[pos_idx[axis], axis] - expected[neg_idx[axis], axis]            actual_range = pos_val - neg_val                        scale[axis] = expected_range / actual_range if actual_range != 0 else 1                return {            'offset': offset,            'scale': scale        }        async def _calibrate_gyroscope(self) -> dict:        """כיול ג'ירו — ממוצע דגימות סטטי"""        logger.info("מתחיל כיול ג'ירו...")        logger.info("השאר את הרחפן ללא תנועה!")                await asyncio.sleep(3)  # ודא יציבות                samples = []        for i in range(self.GYRO_SAMPLES):            gyro = await self.drone.sensors.get_gyroscope()            samples.append(gyro)                        if i % 100 == 0:                logger.info(f"  דגימה {i}/{self.GYRO_SAMPLES}")                        await asyncio.sleep(0.01)                samples = np.array(samples)        offset = np.mean(samples, axis=0)        noise = np.std(samples, axis=0)                logger.info(f"Offset ג'ירו: {offset}")        logger.info(f"רעש ג'ירו: {noise}")                # בדוק אם הרעש סביר        if np.any(noise > 0.1):  # rad/s            logger.warning("רעש גבוה — בדוק רעידות!")                return {            'offset': offset,            'noise': noise        }        async def _calibrate_magnetometer(self) -> dict:        """כיול מצפן — סיבוב בכל הצירים"""        logger.info("מתחיל כיול מצפן...")        logger.info("סובב את הרחפן בכל הצירים!")                samples = []        duration = 30  # שניות                start = asyncio.get_event_loop().time()        while asyncio.get_event_loop().time() - start < duration:            mag = await self.drone.sensors.get_magnetometer()            samples.append(mag)            await asyncio.sleep(0.05)                samples = np.array(samples)                # חשב hard iron (offset)        hard_iron = np.mean(samples, axis=0)                # חשב soft iron (אליפסoid)        centered = samples - hard_iron                # SVD לאליפסoid        U, S, Vt = np.linalg.svd(centered.T @ centered)                # soft iron = התאמת סקאלה        soft_iron = U @ np.diag(1.0 / np.sqrt(S / len(samples))) @ U.T                logger.info(f"Hard iron: {hard_iron}")        logger.info(f"Soft iron:\n{soft_iron}")                return {            'hard_iron': hard_iron,            'soft_iron': soft_iron        }        async def _save_calibration(self, data: IMUCalibrationData):        """שמור כיול"""        # שמור בזיכרון רחפן        await self.drone.sensors.set_calibration(data)                # שמור גם מקומית לגיבוי        import json        backup = {            'accel_offset': data.accel_offset.tolist(),            'accel_scale': data.accel_scale.tolist(),            'gyro_offset': data.gyro_offset.tolist(),            'mag_hard_iron': data.mag_hard_iron.tolist(),            'mag_soft_iron': data.mag_soft_iron.tolist(),            'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat()        }                with open(f"./calibrations/{self.drone.id}_imu.json", 'w') as f:            json.dump(backup, f, indent=2)        async def verify_calibration(self) -> dict:        """בדוק איכות כיול"""        # קרא חיישנים        accel = await self.drone.sensors.get_accelerometer()        gyro = await self.drone.sensors.get_gyroscope()        mag = await self.drone.sensors.get_magnetometer()                # בדוק תאוצה — צריך להיות ~9.81 כששטוח        accel_magnitude = np.linalg.norm(accel)        accel_error = abs(accel_magnitude - 9.81)                # בדוק ג'ירו — צריך להיות ~0 כששטוח        gyro_magnitude = np.linalg.norm(gyro)                # בדוק מצפן — צריך להיות יציב        mag_magnitude = np.linalg.norm(mag)                results = {            'accel_error_g': accel_error / 9.81,            'gyro_drift_deg_s': np.degrees(gyro_magnitude),            'mag_stability': mag_magnitude,            'passed': (                accel_error < 0.5 and  # < 5% שגיאה                gyro_magnitude < 0.01 and  # < 0.5 deg/s                20 < mag_magnitude < 80  # שדה מגנטי סביר            )        }                return results        async def temperature_compensation(self,              temp_data = []        for temp in temperatures:            # המתן לאיזון טמפרטורה            logger.info(f"ממתין ל-{temp}°C...")            await asyncio.sleep(300)  # 5 דקות temp_data41. מערכת ניתוח רעש ואקוסטיקה# skycore/audio/analysis.pyimport numpy as npfrom scipy import signalfrom scipy.fft import fft, fftfreqfrom dataclasses import dataclassfrom typing import List, Tuple, Optionalimport logginglogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)@dataclassclass AcousticSignature:    """חתימה אקוסטית של רחפן"""    fundamental_freq: float          # תדר יסודי מנוע    harmonics: List[float]          # הרמוניות    blade_pass_frequency: float      # תדר מעבר להב    noise_floor_db: float    vibration_spectrum: np.ndarrayclass AcousticAnalyzer:    """מנתח אקוסטיקה ורעש רחפן"""        # תדרים אופייניים    MOTOR_RPM_RANGE = (4000, 25000)  # RPM    BLADE_COUNT = 2                  # מספר להבים למנוע        def __init__(self, sample_rate: int = 44100):        self.sample_rate = sample_rate        self._history: List[AcousticSignature] = []        def analyze_recording(self, audio: np.ndarray) -> AcousticSignature:        """נתח הקלטה אקוסטית"""        # 1. חלון FFT        n = len(audio)        window = signal.windows.hann(n)        audio_windowed = audio * window                # 2. ספקטרום תדרים        spectrum = np.abs(fft(audio_windowed))        freqs = fftfreq(n, 1/self.sample_rate)                # 3. מצא פיקים        peaks, properties = signal.find_peaks(            spectrum[:n//2],            height=np.max(spectrum) * 0.1,            distance=50        )                peak_freqs = freqs[peaks]        peak_amplitudes = spectrum[peaks]                # 4. זהה תדר יסודי        if len(peak_freqs) > 0:            fundamental = peak_freqs[np.argmax(peak_amplitudes)]        else:            fundamental = 0                # 5. הרמוניות        harmonics = []        if fundamental > 0:            for i in range(2, 6):                harmonic = fundamental * i                # מצא את הקרוב ביותר                idx = np.argmin(np.abs(peak_freqs - harmonic))                if abs(peak_freqs[idx] - harmonic) < 10:  # 10 Hz סבילות                    harmonics.append(peak_freqs[idx])                # 6. תדר מעבר להב        blade_pass = fundamental * self.BLADE_COUNT if fundamental > 0 else 0                # 7. רצפת רעש        noise_floor = 20 * np.log10(np.mean(spectrum))                signature = AcousticSignature(            fundamental_freq=fundamental,            harmonics=harmonics,            blade_pass_frequency=blade_pass,            noise_floor_db=noise_floor,            vibration_spectrum=spectrum[:n//2]        )                self._history.append(signature)        return signature        def detect_anomaly(self, current: AcousticSignature) -> List[str]:        """זהה אנומליות לעומת היסטוריה"""        if len(self._history) < 10:            return ["אין מספיק היסטוריה"]                # ממוצע היסטורי        avg_fundamental = np.mean([s.fundamental_freq for s in self._history[:-1]])        std_fundamental = np.std([s.fundamental_freq for s in self._history[:-1]])                issues = []                # בדוק שינוי תדר        if abs(current.fundamental_freq - avg_fundamental) > 2 * std_fundamental:            if current.fundamental_freq > avg_fundamental:                issues.append("תדר מנוע גבוה מהרגיל — בדוק עומס")            else:                issues.append("תדר מנוע נמוך מהרגיל — בדוק סוללה/חום")                # בדוק הרמוניות חדשות        expected_harmonics = set(self._history[0].harmonics)        current_harmonics = set(current.harmonics)                new_harmonics = current_harmonics - expected_harmonics        if new_harmonics:            issues.append(f"הרמוניות חדשות: {new_harmonics} — בדוק שחיקה מכנית")                # בדוק עלייה ברעש        avg_noise = np.mean([s.noise_floor_db for s in self._history[:-1]])        if current.noise_floor_db > avg_noise + 5:            issues.append("רעש גבוה — בדוק מנועים/הילוכים")                return issues        def estimate_motor_health(self, signature: AcousticSignature) -> dict:        """הערך בריאות מנוע מתדרים"""        # המר RPM לתדר        rpm = signature.fundamental_freq * 60                health = {            'rpm': rpm,            'balance_score': 100,            'bearing_condition': 'unknown',            'recommended_action': 'none'        }                # בדוק איזון        if len(signature.harmonics) >= 2:            h2_amplitude = self._get_amplitude_at_freq(signature.harmonics[0])            h1_amplitude = self._get_amplitude_at_freq(signature.fundamental_freq)                        if h2_amplitude / h1_amplitude > 0.3:                health['balance_score'] -= 30                health['recommended_action'] = 'balance_propellers'                # בדוק מיסבים (bearing)        # תדרים גבוהים > 5kHz מצביעים על מיסבים        high_freq_energy = np.sum(signature.vibration_spectrum[5000:])        if high_freq_energy > np.mean(signature.vibration_spectrum) * 10:            health['bearing_condition'] = 'degraded'            health['recommended_action'] = 'inspect_bearings'                return health        def _get_amplitude_at_freq(self, freq: float) -> float:        # stub — צריך גישה לספקטרום המקורי        return 0.0class PropellerBalancer:    """מאזן מדחפים אקוסטית"""        def __init__(self, analyzer: AcousticAnalyzer):        self.analyzer = analyzer        async def balance_procedure(self, drone):        """תהליך איזון אוטומטי"""        logger.info("מתחיל איזון מדחפים...")                # 1. מדידה ראשונית        await drone.motors.set_individual([1000, 0, 0, 0])  # מנוע 1 בלבד        await asyncio.sleep(2)                audio1 = await self._record_motor(drone, 1)        sig1 = self.analyzer.analyze_recording(audio1)                # 2. חזור על כל המנועים        signatures = []        for motor in range(1, 5):            await drone.motors.set_individual(                [1000 if i == motor-1 else 0 for i in range(4)]            )            await asyncio.sleep(2)                        audio = await self._record_motor(drone, motor)            sig = self.analyzer.analyze_recording(audio)            signatures.append(sig)                # 3. השווה        fundamentals = [s.fundamental_freq for s in signatures]        avg_f = np.mean(fundamentals)                imbalances = []        for i, f in enumerate(fundamentals):            deviation = (f - avg_f) / avg_f * 100            imbalances.append({                'motor': i+1,                'deviation_percent': deviation,                'action': 'add_tape' if deviation > 2 else 'none'            })                # 4. המלצות        logger.info("תוצאות איזון:")        for imb in imbalances:            logger.info(f"  מנוע {imb['motor']}: {imb['deviation_percent']:.1f}% — {imb['action']}")                return imbalances        async def _record_motor(self, drone, motor_id: int) -> np.ndarray:        """הקלט מנוע ספציפי"""        # TODO: אינטגרציה עם מיקרופון        # כרגע — מדומה        return np.random.randn(44100) * 0.142. מערכת חיזוי תחזוקה (Predictive Maintenance)# skycore/maintenance/predictor.pyfrom dataclasses import dataclassfrom datetime import datetime, timedeltafrom typing import List, Dict, Optional, Tupleimport numpy as npfrom collections import dequeimport logginglogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)@dataclassclass ComponentHealth:    """בריאות רכיב"""    component: str              # motor_1, battery, gimbal, etc.    health_percent: float       # 0-100    estimated_life_cycles: int  # מחזורים נותרים    failure_probability: float  # 0-1    recommended_action: str    urgency: str               # low, medium, high, criticalclass PredictiveMaintenance:    """חיזוי תחזוקה מבוסס נתונים"""        # קבועי בלאי    MOTOR_LIFETIME_HOURS = 500    BATTERY_CYCLE_LIFETIME = 300    PROPELLER_LIFETIME_HOURS = 50    GIMBAL_MOTOR_LIFETIME = 1000        def __init__(self):        self._flight_history: deque = deque(maxlen=1000)        self._component_usage: Dict[str, dict] = {}        def record_flight(self, flight_data: dict):        """רשום טיסה להיסטוריה"""        self._flight_history.append({            'timestamp': flight_data['start_time'],            'duration_min': flight_data['duration_min'],            'max_throttle': flight_data.get('max_throttle_percent', 0),            'temperature_max': flight_data.get('max_temperature_c', 0),            'vibration_rms': flight_data.get('vibration_rms', 0),            'hard_landings': flight_data.get('hard_landings', 0)        })                # עדכן שימוש רכיבים        self._update_component_usage(flight_data)        def _update_component_usage(self, flight: dict):        """עדכן מונה שימוש רכיבים"""        duration = flight['duration_min'] / 60  # שעות                components = {            'motor_1': {'hours': duration, 'cycles': 1},            'motor_2': {'hours': duration, 'cycles': 1},            'motor_3': {'hours': duration, 'cycles': 1},            'motor_4': {'hours': duration, 'cycles': 1},            'battery': {'cycles': 1},            'propellers': {'hours': duration},            'gimbal': {'hours': duration}        }                for comp, usage in components.items():            if comp not in self._component_usage:                self._component_usage[comp] = {                    'total_hours': 0,                    'total_cycles': 0,                    'stress_score': 0                }                        if 'hours' in usage:                self._component_usage[comp]['total_hours'] += usage['hours']            if 'cycles' in usage:                self._component_usage[comp]['total_cycles'] += usage['cycles']                # חשב stress score        stress = self._calculate_stress(flight)        for comp in components:            self._component_usage[comp]['stress_score'] += stress        def _calculate_stress(self, flight: dict) -> float:        """חשב מקדם מאמץ מהטיסה"""        stress = 1.0  # baseline                # מאמץ מנוע        if flight.get('max_throttle_percent', 0) > 80:            stress *= 1.5                # חום        if flight.get('max_temperature_c', 0) > 50:            stress *= 1.3                # רעידות        if flight.get('vibration_rms', 0) > 5:            stress *= 1.4                # נחיתה קשה        stress *= (1 + flight.get('hard_landings', 0) * 0.5)                return stress        def predict_all_components(self) -> List[ComponentHealth]:        """חזה מצב כל הרכיבים"""        predictions = []                for comp, usage in self._component_usage.items():            health = self._predict_component(comp, usage)            predictions.append(health)                return sorted(predictions, key=lambda x: x.health_percent)        def _predict_component(self, name: str, usage: dict) -> ComponentHealth:        """חזה מצב רכיב בודד"""        if 'motor' in name:            return self._predict_motor(name, usage)        elif name == 'battery':            return self._predict_battery(usage)        elif name == 'propellers':            return self._predict_propellers(usage)        elif name == 'gimbal':            return self._predict_gimbal(usage)                return ComponentHealth(            component=name,            health_percent=50,            estimated_life_cycles=0,            failure_probability=0.5,            recommended_action="inspect",            urgency="medium"        )        def _predict_motor(self, name: str, usage: dict) -> ComponentHealth:        """חזה מצב מנוע"""        hours = usage['total_hours']        stress = usage['stress_score']        cycles = usage['total_cycles']                # בריאות לינארית עם מאמץ        base_health = max(0, 100 - (hours / self.MOTOR_LIFETIME_HOURS) * 100)        stress_factor = max(0.5, 1 - (stress / cycles) * 0.1)                health = base_health * stress_factor                # הסתברות כשל — Weibull פשוט        failure_prob = 1 - np.exp(-(hours / self.MOTOR_LIFETIME_HOURS)**3)                if health > 80:            action, urgency = "none", "low"        elif health > 60:            action, urgency = "inspect", "medium"        elif health > 40:            action, urgency = "service_soon", "high"        else:            action, urgency = "replace_now", "critical"                return ComponentHealth(            component=name,            health_percent=health,            estimated_life_cycles=int((self.MOTOR_LIFETIME_HOURS - hours) * 10),            failure_probability=failure_prob,            recommended_action=action,            urgency=urgency        )        def _predict_battery(self, usage: dict) -> ComponentHealth:        """חזה מצב סוללה"""        cycles = usage['total_cycles']                # בריאות סוללה — מחזורים        health = max(0, 100 - (cycles / self.BATTERY_CYCLE_LIFETIME) * 100)                # בדוק מגמת ירידה        if len(self._flight_history) >= 10:            recent = list(self._flight_history)[-10:]            voltages = [f.get('end_voltage', 0) for f in recent]                        if len(voltages) >= 2:                trend = np.polyfit(range(len(voltages)), voltages, 1)[0]                if trend < -0.05:  # ירידה חדה                    health *= 0.8                failure_prob = cycles / self.BATTERY_CYCLE_LIFETIME                if health > 70:            action, urgency = "monitor", "low"        elif health > 50:            action, urgency = "plan_replacement", "medium"        else:            action, urgency = "replace_soon", "high"                return ComponentHealth(            component="battery",            health_percent=health,            estimated_life_cycles=self.BATTERY_CYCLE_LIFETIME - cycles,            failure_probability=failure_prob,            recommended_action=action,            urgency=urgency        )        def _predict_propellers(self, usage: dict) -> ComponentHealth:        """חזה מצב מדחפים"""        hours = usage['total_hours']                # מדחפים — בלאי מהיר יותר        health = max(0, 100 - (hours / self.PROPELLER_LIFETIME_HOURS) * 100)                # בדוק נזק ויזואלי (אם יש נתונים)        # TODO: אינטגרציה עם בדיקת תמונה                if health > 80:            action, urgency = "inspect_regularly", "low"        else:            action, urgency = "replace", "medium"                return ComponentHealth(            component="propellers",            health_percent=health,            estimated_life_cycles=int(self.PROPELLER_LIFETIME_HOURS - hours),            failure_probability=0.1 if health > 50 else 0.4,            recommended_action=action,            urgency=urgency        )        def _predict_gimbal(self, usage: dict) -> ComponentHealth:        """חזה מצב ג'ימבל"""        hours = usage['total_hours']                health = max(0, 100 - (hours / self.GIMBAL_MOTOR_LIFETIME) * 100)                # בדוק תקלות היסטוריות        gimbal_errors = sum(            1 for f in self._flight_history            if f.get('gimbal_error', False)        )                if gimbal_errors > 3:            health *= 0.7                return ComponentHealth(            component="gimbal",            health_percent=health,            estimated_life_cycles=int(self.GIMBAL_MOTOR_LIFETIME - hours),            failure_probability=0.05,            recommended_action="service_if_jerky",            urgency="low" if health > 70 else "medium"        )        def generate_maintenance_schedule(self) -> List[dict]:        """צור לוח זמנים תחזוקה"""        predictions = self.predict_all_components()                schedule = []        now = datetime.now()                for pred in predictions:            if pred.urgency == "critical":                due = now + timedelta(days=1)            elif pred.urgency == "high":                due = now + timedelta(days=7)            elif pred.urgency == "medium":                due = now + timedelta(days=30)            else:                due = now + timedelta(days=90)                        schedule.append({                'component': pred.component,                'action': pred.recommended_action,                'due_date': due.isoformat(),                'health_percent': pred.health_percent,                'estimated_cost_usd': self._estimate_cost(pred.component, pred.recommended_action)            })                return sorted(schedule, key=lambda x: x['due_date'])        def _estimate_cost(self, component: str, action: str) -> float:        """הערך עלות תחזוקה"""        costs = {            'motor_1': {'replace_now': 80, 'service_soon': 40, 'inspect': 0},            'motor_2': {'replace_now': 80, 'service_soon': 40, 'inspect': 0},            'motor_3': {'replace_now': 80, 'service_soon': 40, 'inspect': 0},            'motor_4': {'replace_now': 80, 'service_soon': 40, 'inspect': 0},            'battery': {'replace_soon': 150, 'plan_replacement': 0, 'monitor': 0},            'propellers': {'replace': 30, 'inspect_regularly': 0},            'gimbal': {'service_if_jerky': 200}        }                return costs.get(component, {}).get(action, 0)43. מערכת אימות בלוקצ’יין ללוגי טיסה (Blockchain Verification)# skycore/blockchain/verifier.pyimport hashlibimport jsonfrom datetime import datetimefrom typing import List, Dict, Optionalfrom dataclasses import dataclass@dataclassclass FlightBlock:    """בלוק בשרשרת לוגי טיסה"""    index: int    timestamp: str    flight_data: dict    previous_hash: str    hash: str    nonce: int = 0        def calculate_hash(self) -> str:        """חשב hash הבלוק"""        block_string = json.dumps({            'index': self.index,            'timestamp': self.timestamp,            'flight_data': self.flight_data,            'previous_hash': self.previous_hash,            'nonce': self.nonce        }, sort_keys=True)                return hashlib.sha256(block_string.encode()).hexdigest()        def mine_block(self, difficulty: int = 4):        """כריית בלוק (Proof of Work פשוט)"""        target = "0" * difficulty                while self.hash[:difficulty] != target:            self.nonce += 1            self.hash = self.calculate_hash()                print(f"בלוק כורה: {self.hash}")class FlightBlockchain:    """שרשרת בלוקים לאימות לוגי טיסה"""        def __init__(self):        self.chain: List[FlightBlock] = []        self.difficulty = 4        self._create_genesis_block()        def _create_genesis_block(self):        """צור בלוק ראשון"""        genesis = FlightBlock(            index=0,            timestamp=datetime.now().isoformat(),            flight_data={"message": "Genesis Block"},            previous_hash="0",            hash=""        )        genesis.hash = genesis.calculate_hash()        self.chain.append(genesis)        def add_flight(self, flight_data: dict) -> FlightBlock:        """הוסף טיסה לשרשרת"""        previous_block = self.chain[-1]                new_block = FlightBlock(            index=len(self.chain),            timestamp=datetime.now().isoformat(),            flight_data=flight_data,            previous_hash=previous_block.hash,            hash=""        )                new_block.mine_block(self.difficulty)        self.chain.append(new_block)                return new_block        def is_valid(self) -> bool:        """בדוק תקינות השרשרת"""        for i in range(1, len(self.chain)):            current = self.chain[i]            previous = self.chain[i-1]                        # בדוק hash            if current.hash != current.calculate_hash():                return False                        # בדוק קשר            if current.previous_hash != previous.hash:                return False                return True        def get_flight_history(self, flight_id: str) -> List[Dict]:        """קבל היסטוריה של טיסה ספציפית"""        return [            block.flight_data            for block in self.chain            if block.flight_data.get('flight_id') == flight_id        ]        def verify_integrity(self, flight_id: str, claimed_data: dict) -> bool:        """אמת שלמות נתוני טיסה"""        history = self.get_flight_history(flight_id)                if not history:            return False                # חשב hash של הנתונים המוצהרים        claimed_hash = hashlib.sha256(            json.dumps(claimed_data, sort_keys=True).encode()        ).hexdigest()                # בדוק מול השרשרת        for record in history:            record_hash = hashlib.sha256(                json.dumps(record, sort_keys=True).encode()            ).hexdigest()                        if record_hash == claimed_hash:                return True                return False        def export_to_file(self, path: str):        """ייצא שרשרת לקובץ"""        export_data = []        for block in self.chain:            export_data.append({                'index': block.index,                'timestamp': block.timestamp,                'flight_data': block.flight_data,                'previous_hash': block.previous_hash,                'hash': block.hash,                'nonce': block.nonce            })                with open(path, 'w') as f:            json.dump(export_data, f, indent=2)        def import_from_file(self, path: str):        """ייבא שרשרת מקובץ"""        with open(path, 'r') as f:            data = json.load(f)                self.chain = []        for item in data:            block = FlightBlock(**item)            self.chain.append(block)                # בדוק תקינות        if not self.is_valid():            raise ValueError("שרשרת מיובאת לא תקינה!")# שימוש לאימות רגולטוריclass RegulatoryCompliance:    """עמידה בדרישות רגולטוריות"""        def __init__(self):        self.blockchain = FlightBlockchain()        def record_flight_for_compliance(self, flight_data: dict):        """רשום טיסה לאימות רגולטורי"""        # הוסף מטא-דאטה נדרש        compliance_data = {            'flight_id': flight_data['flight_id'],            'pilot_id': flight_data['pilot_id'],            'pilot_cert_number': flight_data.get('cert_number'),            'drone_serial': flight_data['drone_serial'],            'drone_registration': flight_data.get('registration'),            'start_time': flight_data['start_time'],            'end_time': flight_data['end_time'],            'max_altitude_m': flight_data['max_altitude_m'],            'max_distance_m': flight_data['max_distance_m'],            'flight_path': flight_data.get('waypoints', []),            'remote_id_log': flight_data.get('remote_id', []),            'operator_location': flight_data.get('operator_location'),            'weather_conditions': flight_data.get('weather'),            'mission_type': flight_data.get('mission_type'),            'airspace_authorization': flight_data.get('authorization')        }                block = self.blockchain.add_flight(compliance_data)                # שמור גם בענן רגולטורי (אם נדרש)        # TODO: אינטגרציה עם מערכות רשות תעופה                return block.hash        def generate_compliance_report(        self,        start_date: datetime,        end_date: datetime,        pilot_id: Optional[str] = None    ) -> dict:        """צור דוח עמידה ברגולציה"""        flights = []                for block in self.blockchain.chain[1:]:  # דל genesis            flight_time = datetime.fromisoformat(block.flight_data['start_time'])                        if start_date <= flight_time <= end_date:                if pilot_id is None or block.flight_data['pilot_id'] == pilot_id:                    flights.append(block.flight_data)                # בדוק עמידה        violations = []        for flight in flights:            if flight['max_altitude_m'] > 120:                violations.append({                    'flight_id': flight['flight_id'],                    'violation': 'altitude_limit',                    'value': flight['max_altitude_m'],                    'limit': 120                })                        # בדוק מרחק VLOS (Visual Line of Sight)            if flight.get('max_distance_m', 0) > 500 and not flight.get('bvlos_authorized'):                violations.append({                    'flight_id': flight['flight_id'],                    'violation': 'vlos_limit',                    'value': flight['max_distance_m'],                    'limit': 500                })                return {            'period': {                'start': start_date.isoformat(),                'end': end_date.isoformat()            },            'total_flights': len(flights),            'total_hours': sum(                (datetime.fromisoformat(f['end_time']) -                  datetime.fromisoformat(f['start_time'])).total_seconds() / 3600                for f in flights            ),            'violations': violations,            'violation_count': len(violations),            'compliance_rate': (len(flights) - len(violations)) / len(flights) * 100 if flights else 100,            'blockchain_integrity': self.blockchain.is_valid()        }44. מערכת סימולציה מזג אוויר מתקדמת# skycore/weather/advanced.pyimport requestsimport numpy as npfrom dataclasses import dataclassfrom datetime import datetime, timedeltafrom typing import List, Dict, Optional, Tupleimport logginglogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)@dataclassclass AtmosphericConditions:    """תנאי אטמוספירה"""    temperature_c: float          # טמפרטורה    pressure_hpa: float           # לחץ    humidity_percent: float       # לחות    wind_speed_ms: float          # מהירות רוח    wind_direction_deg: float     # כיוון רוח    wind_gust_ms: float           # משבי רוח    visibility_km: float          # ראות    cloud_cover_percent: float    # כיסוי עננים    precipitation_mm_h: float     # משקעים    dew_point_c: float            # נקודת טל    turbulence_index: float       # אינדקס טורבולנציה    icing_risk: str               # סיכון קרח: none, light, moderate, severeclass WeatherSimulator:    """סימולטור מזג אוויר לתרגול"""        def __init__(self, base_conditions: Optional[AtmosphericConditions] = None):        self.base = base_conditions or self._default_conditions()        self._time = datetime.now()        self._trend_duration = timedelta(hours=2)        def _default_conditions(self) -> AtmosphericConditions:        """תנאי ברירת מחדל — יום נאה"""        return AtmosphericConditions(            temperature_c=25,            pressure_hpa=1013,            humidity_percent=50,            wind_speed_ms=5,            wind_direction_deg=180,            wind_gust_ms=7,            visibility_km=10,            cloud_cover_percent=20,            precipitation_mm_h=0,            dew_point_c=15,            turbulence_index=0.1,            icing_risk="none"        )        def simulate_scenario(self, scenario: str, intensity: float = 1.0) -> AtmosphericConditions:        """סימולציית תרחיש מזג אוויר"""        scenarios = {            'sudden_wind': self._sudden_wind_change,            'microburst': self._microburst,            'thermal': self._thermal_activity,            'front_passage': self._cold_front,            'fog': self._fog_formation,            'icing': self._icing_conditions,            'dust_devil': self._dust_devil,            'mountain_wave': self._mountain_wave        }                if scenario not in scenarios:            raise ValueError(f"תרחיש לא ידוע: {scenario}")                return scenarios[scenario](intensity)        def _sudden_wind_change(self, intensity: float) -> AtmosphericConditions:        """שינוי רוח פתאומי"""        base = self.base                # רוח עולה פתאום        new_wind = base.wind_speed_ms + 15 * intensity        gust = new_wind * 1.5                # כיוון משתנה        direction_change = np.random.uniform(-60, 60)                return AtmosphericConditions(            temperature_c=base.temperature_c,            pressure_hpa=base.pressure_hpa - 5 * intensity,            humidity_percent=base.humidity_percent,            wind_speed_ms=new_wind,            wind_direction_deg=(base.wind_direction_deg + direction_change) % 360,            wind_gust_ms=gust,            visibility_km=base.visibility_km,            cloud_cover_percent=base.cloud_cover_percent,            precipitation_mm_h=base.precipitation_mm_h,            dew_point_c=base.dew_point_c,            turbulence_index=0.5 * intensity,            icing_risk=base.icing_risk        )        def _microburst(self, intensity: float) -> AtmosphericConditions:        """מיקרוברסט — זרימה נורדת מסוכנת"""        return AtmosphericConditions(            temperature_c=self.base.temperature_c + 2,            pressure_hpa=self.base.pressure_hpa + 10,            humidity_percent=90,            wind_speed_ms=25 * intensity,  # רוח נורדת חזקה            wind_direction_deg=self.base.wind_direction_deg,            wind_gust_ms=35 * intensity,            visibility_km=2,            cloud_cover_percent=80,            precipitation_mm_h=5 * intensity,            dew_point_c=self.base.dew_point_c,            turbulence_index=0.9 * intensity,            icing_risk="none"        )        def _thermal_activity(self, intensity: float) -> AtmosphericConditions:        """פעילות תרמית — טרמיקס"""        # רוח משתנה במרחב — אנומלי בגובה        return AtmosphericConditions(            temperature_c=self.base.temperature_c + 5 * intensity,            pressure_hpa=self.base.pressure_hpa,            humidity_percent=40,            wind_speed_ms=3 + np.random.uniform(-2, 2),            wind_direction_deg=self.base.wind_direction_deg,            wind_gust_ms=8 * intensity,            visibility_km=10,            cloud_cover_percent=10,            precipitation_mm_h=0,            dew_point_c=self.base.dew_point_c,            turbulence_index=0.6 * intensity,            icing_risk="none"        )        def _cold_front(self, intensity: float) -> AtmosphericConditions:        """מעבר חזית קרה"""        return AtmosphericConditions(            temperature_c=self.base.temperature_c - 10 * intensity,            pressure_hpa=self.base.pressure_hpa + 15,            humidity_percent=70,            wind_speed_ms=20 * intensity,            wind_direction_deg=(self.base.wind_direction_deg + 90) % 360,            wind_gust_ms=30 * intensity,            visibility_km=5,            cloud_cover_percent=90,            precipitation_mm_h=2 * intensity,            dew_point_c=self.base.dew_point_c - 5,            turbulence_index=0.7 * intensity,            icing_risk="light" if self.base.temperature_c < 5 else "none"        )        def _fog_formation(self, intensity: float) -> AtmosphericConditions:        """היווצרות ערפל"""        return AtmosphericConditions(            temperature_c=self.base.dew_point_c,            pressure_hpa=self.base.pressure_hpa,            humidity_percent=100,            wind_speed_ms=1,            wind_direction_deg=self.base.wind_direction_deg,            wind_gust_ms=2,            visibility_km=0.1 + 0.4 * (1 - intensity),  # 100m - 500m            cloud_cover_percent=100,            precipitation_mm_h=0,            dew_point_c=self.base.dew_point_c,            turbulence_index=0.05,            icing_risk="none"        )        def _icing_conditions(self, intensity: float) -> AtmosphericConditions:        """תנאי קרח"""        return AtmosphericConditions(            temperature_c=-5 - 5 * intensity,            pressure_hpa=self.base.pressure_hpa,            humidity_percent=85,            wind_speed_ms=15,            wind_direction_deg=self.base.wind_direction_deg,            wind_gust_ms=20,            visibility_km=3,            cloud_cover_percent=100,            precipitation_mm_h=0,            dew_point_c=-7,            turbulence_index=0.4,            icing_risk="severe" if intensity > 0.7 else "moderate"        )        def _dust_devil(self, intensity: float) -> AtmosphericConditions:        """שביב אבק"""        return AtmosphericConditions(            temperature_c=self.base.temperature_c + 3,            pressure_hpa=self.base.pressure_hpa - 3,            humidity_percent=20,            wind_speed_ms=15 * intensity,            wind_direction_deg=np.random.uniform(0, 360),            wind_gust_ms=25 * intensity,            visibility_km=1,            cloud_cover_percent=0,            precipitation_mm_h=0,            dew_point_c=self.base.dew_point_c,            turbulence_index=0.8 * intensity,            icing_risk="none"        )        def _mountain_wave(self, intensity: float) -> AtmosphericConditions:        """גל הרים (Lee wave)"""        return AtmosphericConditions(            temperature_c=self.base.temperature_c,            pressure_hpa=self.base.pressure_hpa,            humidity_percent=50,            wind_speed_ms=20,  # רוח חזקה בכיוון ההרים            wind_direction_deg=270,  # מערב (לדוגמה)            wind_gust_ms=25,            visibility_km=10,            cloud_cover_percent=40,            precipitation_mm_h=0,            dew_point_c=self.base.dew_point_c,            turbulence_index=0.8 * intensity,            icing_risk="moderate" if self.base.temperature_c < 0 else "none"        )        def interpolate_to_time(self, target_time: datetime) -> AtmosphericConditions:        """אינטרפולציה לזמן נתון"""        # פשוט — בפועל ידרוש מודל מורכב יותר        elapsed = (target_time - self._time).total_seconds()        progress = min(1.0, elapsed / self._trend_duration.total_seconds())                # מעבר חלק        # TODO: אינטרפולציה אמיתית                return self.base        def get_flight_recommendation(self, conditions: AtmosphericConditions) -> Dict:        """קבל המלצות טיסה לתנאים"""        issues = []        recommendation = "approved"                if conditions.wind_speed_ms > 10:            issues.append(f"רוח {conditions.wind_speed_ms:.1f} מ'/ש' — היזהר")                if conditions.wind_gust_ms > conditions.wind_speed_ms * 1.5:            issues.append("משבי רוח חזקים — בדוק יציבות")                if conditions.visibility_km < 3:            issues.append(f"ראות נמוכה {conditions.visibility_km} ק\"מ — VLOS עלול להיפגע")            recommendation = "caution"                if conditions.precipitation_mm_h > 1:            issues.append("משקעים — סיכון למים ברכיבים")            recommendation = "discouraged"                if conditions.turbulence_index > 0.5:            issues.append("טורבולנציה — צפה לתנודות")                if conditions.icing_risk in ["moderate", "severe"]:            issues.append(f"סיכון קרח {conditions.icing_risk} — אסור לטוס!")            recommendation = "prohibited"                if conditions.wind_speed_ms > 20:            recommendation = "prohibited"                return {            'recommendation': recommendation,  # approved, caution, discouraged, prohibited            'issues': issues,            'max_altitude_recommended': 60 if conditions.turbulence_index > 0.3 else 120,            'max_distance_recommended': 300 if conditions.visibility_km < 5 else 500,            'operator_skill_required': "advanced" if conditions.wind_speed_ms > 8 else "standard"        }45.
