Simulator)# skycore/hil/full_simulator.pyimport asyncioimport numpy as npfrom dataclasses import dataclassfrom typing import Dict, List, Optional, Tuple, Callablefrom enum import Enumimport serialimport structimport logginglogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)class HILMode(Enum):    SIL = "software_in_loop"      # סימולציה תוכנה בלבד    PIL = "processor_in_loop"     # מעבד אמיתי, חיישנים מדומים    HIL = "hardware_in_loop"     # בקר טיסה אמיתי, פלטפורמה מדומה    VIL = "vehicle_in_loop"      # רחפן אמיתי, סביבה מדומה@dataclassclass SimulatedSensor:    name: str    update_rate_hz: float    noise_model: Callable  # פונקציית רעש    latency_ms: float    failure_probability: floatclass FullHILSimulator:    "סימולטור HIL מלא"        def __init__(self, mode: HILMode = HILMode.SIL):        self.mode = mode        self._running = False        self._physics = PhysicsEngine()        self._sensors: Dict[str, SimulatedSensor] = {}        self._actuator_outputs: np.ndarray = np.zeros(4)        self._serial_port: Optional[serial.Serial] = None                # מצב רחפן מדומה        self.state = {            'position': np.zeros(3),            'velocity': np.zeros(3),            'attitude': np.zeros(3),            'angular_velocity': np.zeros(3),            'motor_rpms': np.zeros(4)        }                # מצב בקר אמיתי (אם HIL)        self.fc_state = {}        async def initialize(self, serial_port: Optional[str] = None):        "אתחל סימולטור"        if self.mode in [HILMode.HIL, HILMode.PIL]:            if not serial_port:                raise ValueError("נדרש serial port ל-HIL/PIL")                        self._serial_port = serial.Serial(                port=serial_port,                baudrate=921600,                timeout=0.001            )                        logger.info(f"מחובר לבקר טיסה על {serial_port}")                        # חכה לאתחול בקר            await self._wait_for_flight_controller()                self._running = True        logger.info(f"סימולטור HIL אתחול במצב {self.mode.value}")        async def _wait_for_flight_controller(self):        "חכה שבקר הטיסה יהיה מוכן"        for _ in range(100):  # 10 שניות מקסימום            if self._serial_port.in_waiting > 0:                data = self._serial_port.read(self._serial_port.in_waiting)                if b'PX4' in data or b'ArduPilot' in data:                    logger.info("בקר טיסה זוהה")                    return            await asyncio.sleep(0.1)                raise TimeoutError("בקר טיסה לא נענה")        async def run(self):        "הרץ לולאת סימולציה"        loop_time = 1.0 / 1000  # 1 kHz                while self._running:            loop_start = asyncio.get_event_loop().time()                        # 1. קרא פקודות מבקר (אם HIL)            if self.mode in [HILMode.HIL, HILMode.PIL]:                await self._read_from_flight_controller()                        # 2. עדכן פיזיקה            self._update_physics(loop_time)                        # 3. סימלץ חיישנים            sensor_data = self._simulate_sensors()                        # 4. שלח לבקר (אם HIL/PIL)            if self.mode in [HILMode.HIL, HILMode.PIL]:                await self._send_to_flight_controller(sensor_data)                        # 5. שלח לממשק משתמש            await self._update_ui()                        # סנכרון תזמון            elapsed = asyncio.get_event_loop().time() - loop_start            if elapsed < loop_time:                await asyncio.sleep(loop_time - elapsed)        async def _read_from_flight_controller(self):        "קרא פקודות מבקר טיסה אמיתי"        if not self._serial_port:            return                # MAVLink או פרוטוקול מותאם        available = self._serial_port.in_waiting        if available >= 16:  # גודל מינימלי            data = self._serial_port.read(available)                        # פארס פקודות מנוע            self._actuator_outputs = self._parse_mavlink_actuators(data)        def _parse_mavlink_actuators(self, data: bytes) -> np.ndarray:        "פארס פקודות מנוע מ-MAVLink"        # MAVLink ACTUATOR_OUTPUTS message (#375)        # פשוט — חפש signature        outputs = np.zeros(4)                if len(data) < 20:            return outputs                # TODO: פארס אמיתי        return outputs        def _update_physics(self, dt: float):        "עדכן מודל פיזיקה"        # המר פקודות מנוע לכוחות        motor_thrusts = self._actuator_outputs * 10  # N                # כוח ומומנט        forces, moments = self._physics.calculate_forces(            self.state, motor_thrusts        )                # אינטגרציה        self.state = self._physics.integrate(self.state, forces, moments, dt)        def _simulate_sensors(self) -> Dict[str, np.ndarray]:        "סימלץ את כל החיישנים"        data = {}                for name, sensor in self._sensors.items():            # קרא מצב אמיתי            if name == 'imu':                raw = self._get_imu_raw()            elif name == 'gps':                raw = self._get_gps_raw()            elif name == 'mag':                raw = self._get_mag_raw()            elif name == 'baro':                raw = self._get_baro_raw()            else:                continue                        # הוסף רעש            noisy = raw + sensor.noise_model(raw)                        # עכב            data[name] = self.state.get('angular_velocity', np.zeros(3))                return np.concatenate([accel, gyro])        def _get_gps_raw(self) -> np.ndarray:        "קבל נתוני GPS"        pos = self.state['position']                # המר ל-WGS84        lat, lon, alt = self._ned_to_wgs84(pos)                return np.array([lat, lon, alt, 0, 0])  # +velocity        def _get_mag_raw(self) -> np.ndarray:        "קבל נתוני מצפן"        # שדה מגנטי מקומי        mag_field = np.array([0.25, 0, 0.45])  # Gauss                # סובב ל-body frame        attitude = self.state['attitude']        # TODO: מטריצת סיבוב                return mag_field        def _get_baro_raw(self) -> np.ndarray:        "קבל נתוני ברומטר"        altitude = self.state['position'][2]        pressure = 101325 * (1 - 2.25577e-5 * altitude)**5.25588                return np.array([pressure, altitude])        def _ned_to_wgs84(self, ned: np.ndarray) -> Tuple[float, float, float]:        "המר NED ל-WGS84"        # מוצא מוכר        lat0, lon0, alt0 = 32.0853, 34.7818, 0                R = 6371000        lat = lat0 + np.degrees(ned[0] / R)        lon = lon0 + np.degrees(ned[1] / (R * np.cos(np.radians(lat0))))        alt = alt0 - ned[2]                return lat, lon, alt        async def _send_to_flight_controller(self, sensor_data: Dict):        "שלח חיישנים מדומים לבקר"        if not self._serial_port:            return                # בנה MAVLink messages        messages = []                if 'imu' in sensor_data:            msg = self._build_mavlink_imu(sensor_data['imu'])            messages.append(msg)                if 'gps' in sensor_data:            msg = self._build_mavlink_gps(sensor_data['gps'])            messages.append(msg)                # שלח        for msg in messages:            self._serial_port.write(msg)        def _build_mavlink_imu(self, data: np.ndarray) -> bytes:        "בנה הודעת IMU MAVLink"        # HIGHRES_IMU (#105)        # פשוט — stub        return b'\xFD' + b'\x00' * 30        def _build_mavlink_gps(self, data: np.ndarray) -> bytes:        "בנה הודעת GPS MAVLink"        # GPS_RAW_INT (#24)        return b'\xFD' + b'\x00' * 30        async def _update_ui(self):        "עדכן תצוגה"        # TODO: WebSocket ל-dashboard        pass        def add_sensor(self, name: str, sensor: SimulatedSensor):        "הוסף חיישן מדומה"        self._sensors[name] = sensor        def inject_fault(self, sensor_name: str, fault_type: str):        "הזן תקלה לבדיקה"        if sensor_name not in self._sensors:            return                logger.warning(f"תקלה מוזנת: {sensor_name} - {fault_type}")                if fault_type == 'noise_increase':            # הגבר רעש פי 10            original = self._sensors[sensor_name].noise_model            self._sensors[sensor_name].noise_model = lambda x: original(x) * 10                elif fault_type == 'latency':            # הוסף עיכוב 500ms            self._sensors[sensor_name].latency_ms += 500                elif fault_type == 'dropout':            # איבוד דגימות            self._sensors[sensor_name].failure_probability = 0.5        async def run_scenario(self, scenario: Dict):        "הרץ תרחיש בדיקה"        logger.info(f"מתחיל תרחיש: {scenario['name']}")                # אתחל מצב        self.state['position'] = np.array(scenario.get('start_position', [0, 0, 0]))                # הזן תקלות לפי לוח זמנים        for event in scenario.get('events', []):            await asyncio.sleep(event['time_sec'])            self.inject_fault(event['sensor'], event['fault'])                # self._history: List[AirQualityReading] = []        self._sensors: Dict[str, dict] = {}  # רחפנים עם חיישנים        async def get_current_aqi(self, lat: float, lon: float) ->                return AirQualityReading(                timestamp=datetime.now(),                location=(lat, lon, 0),                pm25_ug_m3=result.get('measurements', {}).get('pm25', 0),                pm10_ug_m3=result.get('measurements', {}).get('pm10', 0),                o3_ppb=result.get('measurements', {}).get('o3', 0),                no2_ppb=result.get('measurements', {}).get('no2', 0),                so2_ppb=result.get('measurements', {}).get('so2', 0),                co_ppm=result.get('measurements', {}).get('co', 0),                aqi=self._calculate_aqi(result),                temperature_c=0,                humidity_percent=0            )                    except Exception as e:            logger.error(f"שגיאת AQI: {e}")            return None        def _calculate_aqi(self, data: dict) -> int:        "חשב AQI ממדידות"        # EPA AQI formula פשוט        pm25 = data.get('measurements', {}).get('pm25', 0)                if pm25 <= 12:            return int(pm25 * 50 / 12)        elif pm25 <= 35.4:            return int(50 + (pm25 - 12) * 50 / 23.4)        elif pm25 <= 55.4:            return int(100 + (pm25 - 35.4) * 50 / 20)        elif pm25 <= 150.4:            return int(150 + (pm25 - 55.4) * 50 / 95)        elif pm25 <= 250.4:            return int(200 + (pm25 - 150.4) * 100 / 100)        else:            return min(500, int(300 + (pm25 - 250.4) * 200 / 149.6))        def register_drone_sensor(self, drone_id: str, sensor_type: str):        "רשום רחפן עם חיישן אוויר"        self._sensors[drone_id] = {            'type': sensor_type,            'calibrated': False,            'last_reading': None        }        async def collect_from_drone(self, drone_id: str, telemetry: dict) -> Optional[AirQualityReading]:        "אסוף מדידה מרחפן"        if drone_id not in self._sensors:            return None                # חיישן פיזי על הרחפן        sensor_data = telemetry.get('air_quality', {})                reading = AirQualityReading(            timestamp=datetime.now(),            location=(                telemetry.get('lat', 0),                telemetry.get('lon', 0),                telemetry.get('alt', 0)            ),            pm25_ug_m3=sensor_data.get('pm25', 0),            pm10_ug_m3=sensor_data.get('pm10', 0),            o3_ppb=sensor_data.get('o3', 0),            no2_ppb=sensor_data.get('no2', 0),            so2_ppb=sensor_data.get('so2', 0),            co_ppm=sensor_data.get('co', 0),            aqi=0,  # יחושב            temperature_c=telemetry.get('temperature', 0),            humidity_percent=telemetry.get('humidity', 0)        )                reading.aqi = self._calculate_aqi_from_reading(reading)        self._history.append(reading)                return reading        def _calculate_aqi_from_reading(self, reading: AirQualityReading) -> int:        "חשב AQI מקריאה"        # פשוט — מבוסס PM2.5 בעיקר        pm25 = reading.pm25_ug_m3                if pm25 <= 12:            return int(pm25 * 50 / 12)        elif pm25 <= 35.4:            return int(50 + (pm25 - 12) * 50 / 23.4)        else:            return min(300, int(100 + (pm25 - 35.4) * 100 / 20))        def get_flight_recommendation(self, aqi: int) -> Dict:        "המלצת טיסה לפי AQI"        levels = {            (0, 50): {                'level': 'Good',                'color': 'green',                'recommendation': 'safe_to_fly',                'precautions': []            },            (51, 100): {                'level': 'Moderate',                'color': 'yellow',                'recommendation': 'acceptable',                'precautions': ['Sensitive individuals should limit exposure']            },            (101, 150): {                'level': 'Unhealthy for Sensitive',                'color': 'orange',                'recommendation': 'caution',                'precautions': ['Reduce flight time', 'Avoid hovering in one area']            },            (151, 200): {                'level': 'Unhealthy',                'color': 'red',                'recommendation': 'avoid',                'precautions': ['Do not fly unless essential', 'Use respiratory protection']            },            (201, 300): {                'level': 'Very Unhealthy',                'color': 'purple',                'recommendation': 'prohibited',                'precautions': ['Flight prohibited by safety guidelines']            },            (301, 500): {                'level': 'Hazardous',                'color': 'maroon',                'recommendation': 'emergency_only',                'precautions': ['Emergency services only']            }        }                for (low, high), info in levels.items():            if low <= aqi <= high:                return {**info, 'aqi': aqi}                return levels[(301, 500)]        def generate_pollution_map(self, area: Dict) -> Dict:        "צור מפת זיהום"        # אסוף כל הקריאות באזור        readings = [            r for r in self._history            if area['south'] <= r.location[0] <= area['north']            and area['west'] <= r.location[1] <= area['east']        ]                # Grid        grid = {}        for r in readings:            key = (round(r.location[0], 3), round(r.location[1], 3))            if key not in grid:                grid[key] = []            grid[key].append(r.pm25_ug_m3)                # ממוצע        return {            'grid_points': [                {                    'lat': k[0],                    'lon': k[1],                    'pm25_avg': np.mean(v),                    'aqi': self._calculate_aqi({'measurements': {'pm25': np.mean(v)}}),                    'readings_count': len(v)                }                for k, v in grid.items()            ],            'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat()        }60. מערכת זיהוי פגיעה בפרטיות (Privacy Protection)# skycore/privacy/protection.pyfrom dataclasses import dataclassfrom datetime import datetimefrom typing import Dict, List, Optional, Set, Tuplefrom enum import Enumimport numpy as npimport logginglogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)class PrivacyZoneType(Enum):    RESIDENTIAL = "residential"      # מגורים    HOSPITAL = "hospital"             # בית חולים    SCHOOL = "school"                 # בית ספר    RELIGIOUS = "religious"           # מקום דתי    MILITARY = "military"            # צבאי    PRIVATE_PROPERTY = "private"       # רכוש פרטי    GLBA = "glba"                     # Gramm-Leach-Bliley (בנקים)    HIPAA = "hipaa"                   # רפואי ארה"ב@dataclassclass PrivacyZone: שעות אסורות    authorized_operators: Optional[List[str]] = None  # מורשיםclass PrivacyProtectionSystem:    "מערכת הגנת פרטיות"        def __init__(self):        self.zones: Dict[str, PrivacyZone] = {}        self._consent_registry: Dict[str, dict] = {}  # consent מבעלי רכוש        self._blur_regions: List[Tuple[int, int, int, int]] = []  # פיקסלים לטשטוש        def register_zone(self, zone: node["amenity"="hospital"]({area['south']},{area['west']},{area['north']},{area['east']});          node["amenity"="school"]({area['south']},{area['west']},{area['north']},{area['east']});          way["building"="residential"]({area['south']},{area['west']},{area['north']},{area['east']});        );        out center;        """                # TODO: שליחה ל-Overpass        pass        def check_flight_plan(self, waypoints: List[Tuple[float, float, float]]) -> Dict:        "בדוק תכנית טיסה מול אזורי פרטיות"        violations = []        warnings = []                for i, wp in enumerate(waypoints):            for zone_id, zone in self.zones.items():                distance = self._haversine(wp[0], wp[1], zone.center[0], zone.center[1])                                if distance < zone.radius_m:                    # בדוק גובה                    if wp[2] < zone.altitude_limit_m:                        # בדוק שעות                        if self._is_time_restricted(zone):                            violations.append({                                'waypoint_index': i,                                'zone_id': zone_id,                                'zone_type': zone.zone_type.value,                                'distance_m': distance,                                'altitude_m': wp[2],                                'restriction': 'time_and_altitude'                            })                        else:                            warnings.append({                                'waypoint_index': i,                                'zone_id': zone_id,                                'message': 'Entering privacy zone during allowed hours'                            })                return {            'approved': len(violations) == 0,            'violations': violations,            'warnings': warnings,            'requires_consent': any(v['zone_type'] == 'private' for v in violations)        }        def _haversine(self, lat1, lon1, lat2, lon2) -> float:        "מרחק בין נקודות"        R = 6371000        phi1, phi2 = np.radians(lat1), np.radians(lat2)        dphi = np.radians(lat2 - lat1)        dlambda = np.radians(lon2 - lon1)                a = np.sin(dphi/2)**2 + np.cos(phi1)*np.cos(phi2)*np.sin(dlambda/2)**2        return 2 * R * np.arcsin(np.sqrt(a))        def _is_time_restricted(self, zone: PrivacyZone) -> bool:        "בדוק אם שעה נוכחית מוגבלת"        if not zone.time_restrictions:            return False                now = datetime.now()        hour = now.hour                for restriction in zone.time_restrictions.get('blocked_hours', []):            if restriction['start'] <= hour <= restriction['end']:                return True                return False        def process_video_frame(self, frame: np.ndarray, metadata: dict) -> np.ndarray:        "עבד פריים וידאו — טשטוש פנים/לוחיות רישוי"        # זיהוי אוטומטי        faces = self._detect_faces(frame)        plates = self._detect_license_plates(frame)                # טשטוש        for (x, y, w, h) in faces:            frame = self._blur_region(frame, x, y, w, h, intensity=15)                for (x, y, w, h) in plates:            frame = self._blur_region(frame, x, y, w, h, intensity=20)                # בדוק אם פריים מכיל אזור פרטיות        if 'gps' in metadata:            for zone in self.zones.values():                dist = self._haversine(                    metadata['gps']['lat'], metadata['gps']['lon'],                    zone.center[0], zone.center[1]                )                                if dist < zone.radius_m and zone.recording_prohibited:                    # מחק פריים                    return np.zeros_like(frame)                return frame        def _detect_faces(self, frame: np.ndarray) -> List[Tuple[int, int, int, int]]:        "זהה פנים"        # TODO: OpenCV DNN או MediaPipe        return []        def _detect_license_plates(self, frame: np.ndarray) -> List[Tuple[int, int, int, int]]:        "זהה לוחיות רישוי"        # TODO: OCR + detection        return []        def _blur_region(self, frame: np.ndarray, x: int, y: int, w: int, h: int, intensity: int) -> np.ndarray:        "טשטוש אזור"        roi = frame[y:y+h, x:x+w]        blurred = cv2.GaussianBlur(roi, (intensity*2+1, intensity*2+1), 0)        frame[y:y+h, x:x+w] = blurred        return frame        def record_consent(self, property_owner: str, drone_id: str, date_range: Tuple[datetime, datetime], restrictions: dict):        "רשם consent מבעל רכוש"        consent_id = f"{property_owner}_{drone_id}_{date_range[0].strftime('%Y%m%d')}"                self._consent_registry[consent_id] = {            'owner': property_owner,            'drone_id': drone_id,            'valid_from': date_range[0],            'valid_to': date_range[1],            'restrictions': restrictions,            'recorded_at': datetime.now()        }                logger.info(f"Consent נרשם: {consent_id}")        def verify_consent(self, property_owner: str, drone_id: str, timestamp: datetime) -> bool:        "אמת consent"        for consent in self._consent_registry.values():            if (consent['owner'] == property_owner and                 consent['drone_id'] == drone_id and                consent['valid_from'] <= timestamp <= consent['valid_to']):                return True                return False        def generate_privacy_report(self, flight_id: str) -> str:        "צור דוח פרטיות"        return f"""# Privacy Compliance Report — Flight {flight_id}## Zones Encountered{chr(10).join(f"- {z.zone_type.value}: {z.radius_m}m radius" for z in self.zones.values())}## Consent Records{len(self._consent_registry)} active consents## Video Processing- Faces blurred: [count]- License plates blurred: [count]- Frames redacted: [count]## Compliance Status{'✓ Compliant' if not any(z.recording_prohibited for z in self.zones.values()) else '⚠ Review Required'}---Generated: {datetime.now().isoformat()}"""61. מערכת תמיכת לקוחות ודיבוג מרחוק (Remote Support)# skycore/support/remote.pyimport asyncioimport jsonfrom dataclasses import dataclassfrom הצללת RF ממבנים"        total_attenuation_db = 0        for building in self.buildings.values():            # בדוק אם קו הראייה חותך את המבנה            intersection = self._line_building_intersection(                tx_pos, rx_pos, building            )            if intersection:                # חשב אטנואציה לפי חומר                material_attenuation = {                    MaterialType.CONCRETE: 15,  # dB                    MaterialType.STEEL: 25,                    MaterialType.GLASS: 3,                    MaterialType.WOOD: 5,                    MaterialType.VEGETATION: 2                }                att = material_attenuation.get(                    building.surface_properties.material, 10                )                # תלות בתדירות                att *= (frequency_ghz / 5.8) ** 2                total_attenuation_db += att        return total_attenuation_db    def _line_building_intersection(        self,        p1: Tuple[float, float, float],        p2: Tuple[float, float, float],        building: Building3D    ) -> Optional[Tuple[float, float, float]]:        "בדוק חיתוך קו עם מבנה"        # Ray-prism intersection פשוט        # המר ל-local        # בדוק אם הקו חותך את ה-footprint        # TODO: geometric intersection        return None    def calculate_thermal_signature(        self,        drone_position: Tuple[float, float, float],        time_of_day: float  # שעות מ-0-24    ) -> float:        "חשב חתימה תרמית של הרחפן מול רקע"        # טמפרטורת רקע        ground_temp = self._get_ground_temperature(drone_position, time_of_day)        # טמפרטורת רחפן (מנועים + אלקטרוניקה)        drone_temp = 40  # °C baseline        # contrast        contrast = abs(drone_temp - ground_temp)        return contrast    def _get_ground_temperature(        self,        pos: Tuple[float, float, float],        hour: float    ) -> float:        "קבל טמפרטורת קרקע"        # מודל פשוט        base_temp = 25        daily_variation = 10 * np.sin(2 * np.pi * (hour - 6) / 24)        # תלות בחומר        material_factor = 1.0        return base_temp + daily_variation * material_factor    def generate_point_cloud(self, density: float = 10.0) -> np.ndarray:        "צור ענן נקודות של הסביבה"        points = []        # מבנים        for building in self.buildings.values():            building_points = self._building_to_points(building, density)            points.extend(building_points)        # טרן        if self.terrain:            terrain_points = self._terrain_to_points(self.terrain, density)            points.extend(terrain_points)        return np.array(points)    def _building_to_points(        self,        building: Building3D,        density: float    ) -> List[Tuple[float, float, float]]:        "המר מבנה לנקודות"        points = []        # קרקע        for x, y in building.footprint:            points.append((x, y, 0))        # גג        for x, y in building.footprint:            points.append((x, y, building.height_m))        # קירות — דגום        n_wall_points = int(building.height_m * density)        for i in range(n_wall_points):            z = i / density            for j in range(len(building.footprint)):                x1, y1 = building.footprint[j]                x2, y2 = building.footprint[(j+1) % len(building.footprint)]                # דגום לאורך הקיר                for t in np.linspace(0, 1, 5):                    points.append((                        x1 + t * (x2 - x1),                        y1 + t * (y2 - y1),                        z                    ))        return points    def _terrain_to_points(        self,        terrain: Terrain3D,        density: float    ) -> List[Tuple[float, float, float]]:        "המר טרן לנקודות"        points = []        h, w = terrain.elevation_map.shape        step = max(1, int(1 / (density * terrain.resolution_m)))        for i in range(0, h, step):            for j in range(0, w, step):                x = j * terrain.resolution_m                y = i * terrain.resolution_m                z = terrain.elevation_map[i, j]                points.append((x, y, z))        return points    def export_to_unity(self, path: str):        "ייצא ל-Unity (סימולטור)"        # TODO: ייצוא mesh + textures    def export_to_gazebo(self, path: str):        "ייצא ל-Gazebo (ROS)"        # TODO: SDF format64. מערכת חיזוי ביצועים אווירודינמיים (Aerodynamic Performance)# skycore/aerodynamics/predictor.pyimport numpy as npfrom dataclasses import dataclassfrom typing import Dict, List, Optional, Tuplefrom enum import Enumimport logginglogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)class AirfoilType(Enum):    SYMMETRIC = "symmetric"      # למסוקים — NACA 0012    CAMBERED = "cambered"        # למטוסים    DELTA = "delta"              # כנפי דלתא@dataclassclass AerodynamicCoefficients:    cl_alpha: float      # שיפוע מקדם עילוי    cd0: float           # מקדם גרר אפס    cd_alpha2: float     # גרר פרופורציונלי לעילוי בריבוע    cm0: float           # מומנט אפס    alpha_stall: float   # זווית אבדה (rad)    cl_max: float        # עילוי מקסימלי@dataclassclass PropellerPerformance:    diameter_m: float    pitch_m: float    blades: int    rpm_max: float    efficiency: float      # 0-1class AerodynamicPredictor:    "חוזה ביצועים אווירודינמיים"    # קבועי אוויר    RHO_SL = 1.225  # kg/m³ at sea level    G = 9.81    def __init__(self, drone_config: dict):        self.mass = drone_config['mass_kg']        self.propellers = drone_config.get('propellers', 4)        self.prop = PropellerPerformance(**drone_config['propeller'])        self.airfoil = AerodynamicCoefficients(**drone_config.get('airfoil', {}))        # גיאומטריה        self.arm_length_m = drone_config.get('arm_length_m', 0.2)        self.drag_area_m2 = drone_config.get('drag_area_m2', 0.05)    def calculate_hover_power(self, altitude_m: float = 0) -> float:        "חשב הספק רחיפה"        rho = self._air_density(altitude_m)        # משקל        weight = self.mass * self.G        # דיסק אקטואטור        disk_area = np.pi * (self.prop.diameter_m / 2) ** 2        total_disk_area = disk_area * self.propellers        # induced velocity        v_i = np.sqrt(weight / (2 * rho * total_disk_area))        # הספק induced        power_induced = weight * v_i / self.prop.efficiency        # הספק profile (פשוט)        power_profile = 0.1 * power_induced  # 10% approximate        return power_induced + power_profile    def calculate_max_speed(self, altitude_m: float = 0) -> float:        "חשב מהירות מקסימלית"        rho = self._air_density(altitude_m)        # available power        power_available = self._max_motor_power() * self.propellers        # drag at speed V: D = 0.5 * rho * V^2 * Cd * A        # power required = D * V = 0.5 * rho * V^3 * Cd * A        # solve for V where power_available = power_required        cd = 0.5  # approximate drag coefficient        a = 0.5 * rho * cd * self.drag_area_m2        # V = (P / a)^(1/3)        v_max = (power_available / a) ** (1/3)        return v_max    def calculate_climb_rate(self, climb_angle_deg: float = 0, altitude_m: float = 0) -> float:        "חשב קצב טיפוס"        # available excess power        power_hover = self.calculate_hover_power(altitude_m)        power_available = self._max_motor_power() * self.propellers        power_excess = power_available - power_hover        # climb power = m * g * climb_rate        # climb_rate = power_excess / (m * g)        climb_rate = power_excess / (self.mass * self.G)        # תלות בזווית        climb_rate *= np.cos(np.radians(climb_angle_deg))        return climb_rate    def calculate_wind_tolerance(self, wind_speed_ms: float, wind_direction_deg: float) -> bool:        "בדוק אם רחפן יכול לעמוד ברוח"        # maximum tilt angle        max_tilt_deg = 45        # required tilt to counter wind        # simplified: tan(tilt) = wind_drag / weight        rho = self.RHO_SL        wind_drag = 0.5 * rho * wind_speed_ms**2 * self.drag_area_m2        required_tilt = np.degrees(np.arctan2(wind_drag, self.mass * self.G))        return required_tilt < max_tilt_deg    def predict_flight_time(        self,        battery_wh: float,        mission_profile: List[Dict]    ) -> float:        "חזה זמן טיסה לפרופיל משימה"        total_energy = battery_wh * 3600  # Joules        for segment in mission_profile:            duration_sec = segment['duration_sec']            speed_ms = segment.get('speed_ms', 0)            altitude_m = segment.get('altitude_m', 0)            if speed_ms == 0:                # רחיפה                power = self.calculate_hover_power(altitude_m)            else:                # טיסה קדמית                power = self._forward_flight_power(speed_ms, altitude_m)            energy = power * duration_sec            total_energy -= energy            if total_energy < 0:                return sum(s['duration_sec'] for s in mission_profile[:mission_profile.index(segment)])        # convert remaining to hover time        hover_power = self.calculate_hover_power(0)        remaining_time = total_energy / hover_power        return sum(s['duration_sec'] for s in mission_profile) + remaining_time    def _air_density(self, altitude_m: float) -> float:        "חשב צפיפות אוויר"        # ISA model        if altitude_m < 11000:            t = 288.15 - 0.0065 * altitude_m            p = 101325 * (t / 288.15) ** 5.25588        else:            t = 216.65            p = 22632 * np.exp(-0.00015768866 * (altitude_m - 11000))        rho = p / (287.05 * t)        return rho    def _max_motor_power(self) -> float:        "הספק מנוע מקסימלי"        # from propeller data        rpm = self.prop.rpm_max        # P = 2π * τ * rpm / 60        # approximate        return 200  # W per motor    def _forward_flight_power(self, speed_ms: float, altitude_m: float) -> float:        "הספק טיסה קדמית"        rho = self._air_density(altitude_m)        # induced power (less than hover due to translational lift)        v_i = self.calculate_hover_power(altitude_m) / (self.mass * self.G)        v_i_forward = v_i * (1 - speed_ms / (2 * v_i))  # simplified        # profile drag        drag = 0.5 * rho * speed_ms**2 * self.drag_area_m2 * 0.5        power_profile = drag * speed_ms        # induced        power_induced = self.mass * self.G * v_i_forward        return power_profile + power_induced    def generate_performance_chart(self) -> Dict:        "צור טבלת ביצועים"        altitudes = np.arange(0, 3000, 500)        temperatures = np.arange(-20, 45, 5)        chart = {}        for alt in altitudes:            chart[int(alt)] = {}            for temp in temperatures:                # תלות טמפרטורה בצפיפות                rho = self._air_density(alt) * (288.15 / (288.15 + temp - 15))                hover_power = self.calculate_hover_power(alt) * (self.RHO_SL / rho)                chart[int(alt)][int(temp)] = {                    'hover_power_w': round(hover_power, 1),                    'max_speed_ms': round(self.calculate_max_speed(alt), 1),                    'climb_rate_ms': round(self.calculate_climb_rate(altitude_m=alt), 1)                }        return chart65. מערכת אופטימיזציית מסלול בזמן אמת (Real-Time Path Optimization)# skycore/planning/rt_optimization.pyimport numpy as npfrom dataclasses import dataclassfrom typing import Dict, List, Optional, Tuple, Setfrom heapq import heappush, heappopimport logginglogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)@dataclassclass Node:    position: Tuple[float, float, float]    g_cost: float  # cost from start    h_cost: float  # heuristic to goal    parent: Optional['Node'] = None    @property    def f_cost(self):        return self.g_cost + self.h_costclass RTOptimizer:    "אופטימיזציית מסלול בזמן אמת"    def __init__(self, grid_resolution_m: float = 5.0):        self.resolution = grid_resolution_m        self._obstacle_grid: Optional[np.ndarray] = None        self._cost_grid: Optional[np.ndarray] = None        self._dynamic_obstacles: Dict[str, Tuple[float, float, float]] = {}    def update_obstacle_map(self, obstacles: List[dict]):        "עדכן מפת מכשולים"        # המר ל-grid        bounds = self._calculate_bounds(obstacles)        nx = int((bounds['x_max'] - bounds['x_min']) / self.resolution) + 1        ny = int((bounds['y_max'] - bounds['y_min']) / self.resolution) + 1        nz = int((bounds['z_max'] - bounds['z_min']) / self.resolution) + 1        grid = np.zeros((nx, ny, nz), dtype=bool)        for obs in obstacles:            # סמן תאים תפוסים            cells = self._obstacle_to_cells(obs, bounds)            for cx, cy, cz in cells:                if 0 <= cx < nx and 0 <= cy < ny and 0 <= cz < nz:                    grid[cx, cy, cz] = True        self._obstacle_grid = grid        self._bounds = bounds    def _calculate_bounds(self, obstacles: List[dict]) -> Dict:        "חשב גבולות"        all_x = []        all_y = []        all_z = []        for obs in obstacles:            x, y, z = obs['position']            r = obs.get('radius', 10)            all_x.extend([x - r, x + r])            all_y.extend([y - r, y + r])            all_z.extend([z - r, z + r])        return {            'x_min': min(all_x), 'x_max': max(all_x),            'y_min': min(all_y), 'y_max': max(all_y),            'z_min': max(0, min(all_z)), 'z_max': max(all_z)        }    def _obstacle_to_cells(        self,        obstacle: dict,        bounds: Dict    ) -> List[Tuple[int, int, int]]:        "המר מכשול לתאי grid"        x, y, z = obstacle['position']        r = obstacle.get('radius', 10)        cx = int((x - bounds['x_min']) / self.resolution)        cy = int((y - bounds['y_min']) / self.resolution)        cz = int((z - bounds['z_min']) / self.resolution)        cells = []        cells_per_radius = int(r / self.resolution) + 1        for dx in range(-cells_per_radius, cells_per_radius + 1):            for dy in range(-cells_per_radius, cells_per_radius + 1):                for dz in range(-cells_per_radius, cells_per_radius + 1):                    if dx**2 + dy**2 + dz**2 <= cells_per_radius**2:                        cells.append((cx + dx, cy + dy, cz + dz))        return cells    def add_dynamic_obstacle(self, obs_id: str, position: Tuple[float, float, float], velocity: Tuple[float, float, float]):        "הוסף מכשול דינמי"        self._dynamic_obstacles[obs_id] = {            'position': position,            'velocity': velocity,            'predicted_positions': self._predict_trajectory(position, velocity)        }    def _predict_trajectory(        self,        position: Tuple[float, float, float],        velocity: Tuple[float, float, float],        horizon_sec: float = 10    ) -> List[Tuple[float, float, float]]:        "חזה מסלול עתידי"        positions = []        dt = 1.0        for t in np.arange(0, horizon_sec, dt):            x = position[0] + velocity[0] * t            y = position[1] + velocity[1] * t            z = position[2] + velocity[2] * t            positions.append((x, y, z))        return positions    def find_path(        self,        start: Tuple[float, float, float],        goal: Tuple[float, float, float],        max_time_ms: float = 100    ) -> Optional[List[Tuple[float, float, float]]]:        "מצא מסלול A* מהיר"        if self._obstacle_grid is None:            return [start, goal]        # המר ל-grid coordinates        start_cell = self._world_to_grid(start)        goal_cell = self._world_to_grid(goal)        # A*        open_set = []        closed_set: Set[Tuple[int, int, int]] = set()        start_node = Node(            position=start_cell,            g_cost=0,            h_cost=self._heuristic(start_cell, goal_cell)        )        heappush(open_set, (start_node.f_cost, id(start_node), start_node))        nodes: Dict[Tuple[int, int, int], Node] = {start_cell: start_node}        start_time = asyncio.get_event_loop().time()        while open_set:            # בדיקת זמן            if (asyncio.get_event_loop().time() - start_time) * 1000 > max_time_ms:                logger.warning("A* timeout — מחזיר מסלול חלקי")                break            _, _, current = heappop(open_set)            if current.position == goal_cell:                # שחזר מסלול                return self._reconstruct_path(current, start, goal)            closed_set.add(current.position)            # שכנים            neighbors = self._get_neighbors(current.position)            for neighbor_pos in neighbors:                if neighbor_pos in closed_set:                    continue                if self._is_occupied(neighbor_pos):                    continue                # בדוק מכשולים דינמיים                if self._collision_with_dynamic(neighbor_pos):                    continue                # cost                move_cost = self._move_cost(current.position, neighbor_pos)                tentative_g = current.g_cost + move_cost                if neighbor_pos not in nodes or tentative_g < nodes[neighbor_pos].g_cost:                    neighbor = Node(                        position=neighbor_pos,                        g_cost=tentative_g,                        h_cost=self._heuristic(neighbor_pos, goal_cell),                        parent=current                    )                    nodes[neighbor_pos] = neighbor                    heappush(open_set, (neighbor.f_cost, id(neighbor), neighbor))        # לא נמצא מסלול מלא        if goal_cell in nodes:            return self._reconstruct_path(nodes[goal_cell], start, goal)        return None    def _world_to_grid(self, pos: Tuple[float, float, float]) -> Tuple[int, int, int]:        "המר מקואורדינטות עולם ל-grid"        cx = int((pos[0] - self._bounds['x_min']) / self.resolution)        cy = int((pos[1] - self._bounds['y_min']) / self.resolution)        cz = int((pos[2] - self._bounds['z_min']) / self.resolution)        return (cx, cy, cz)    def _grid_to_world(self, cell: Tuple[int, int, int]) -> Tuple[float, float, float]:        "המר מ-grid לקואורדינטות עולם"        x = cell[0] * self.resolution + self._bounds['x_min']        y = cell[1] * self.resolution + self._bounds['y_min']        z = cell[2] * self.resolution + self._bounds['z_min']        return (x, y, z)    def _heuristic(self, a: Tuple[int, int, int], b: Tuple[int, int, int]) -> float:        "היוריסטיקה — מרחק אוקלידי"        return np.sqrt(sum((a[i] - b[i])**2 for i in range(3))) * self.resolution    def _get_neighbors(self, cell: Tuple[int, int, int]) -> List[Tuple[int, int, int]]:        "קבל שכנים (26-connectivity)"        neighbors = []        for dx in [-1, 0, 1]:            for dy in [-1, 0, 1]:                for dz in [-1, 0, 1]:                    if dx == 0 and dy == 0 and dz == 0:                        continue                    neighbors.append((cell[0]+dx, cell[1]+dy, cell[2]+dz))        return neighbors    def _is_occupied(self, cell: Tuple[int, int, int]) -> bool:        "בדוק אם תא תפוס"        if self._obstacle_grid is None:            return False        nx, ny, nz = self._obstacle_grid.shape        if not (0 <= cell[0] < nx and 0 <= cell[1] < ny and 0 <= cell[2] < nz):            return True  # out of bounds = occupied        return self._obstacle_grid[cell[0], cell[1], cell[2]]    def _collision_with_dynamic(self, cell: Tuple[int, int, int]) -> bool:        "בדוק התנגשות עם מכשול דינמי"        world_pos = self._grid_to_world(cell)        for obs in self._dynamic_obstacles.values():            for pred_pos in obs['predicted_positions']:                dist = np.sqrt(sum((world_pos[i] - pred_pos[i])**2 for i in range(3)))                if dist < 10:  # 10m safety margin                    return True        return False    def _move_cost(self, a: Tuple[int, int, int], b: Tuple[int, int, int]) -> float:        "עלות תנועה"        # diagonal vs straight        diff = sum(abs(a[i] - b[i]) for i in range(3))        if diff == 1:            return self.resolution  # straight        elif diff == 2:            return self.resolution * np.sqrt(2)  # diagonal 2D        else:            return self.resolution * np.sqrt(3)  # diagonal 3D    def _reconstruct_path(        self,        node: Node,        start_world: Tuple[float, float, float],        goal_world: Tuple[float, float, float]    ) -> List[Tuple[float, float, float]]:        "שחזר מסלול"        path = []        current: Optional[Node] = node        while current:            path.append(self._grid_to_world(current.position))            current = current.parent        path.reverse()        # החלף ראש וסוף עם עולם אמיתי        path[0] = start_world        path[-1] = goal_world        # החלק        return self._smooth_path(path)    def _smooth_path(        self,        path: List[Tuple[float, float, float]],        tolerance: float = 1.0    ) -> List[Tuple[float, float, float]]:        "החלק מסלול — Ramer-Douglas-Peucker"        if len(path) < 3:            return path        def point_line_distance(point, start, end):            if start == end:                return np.linalg.norm(np.array(point) - np.array(start))            line_vec = np.array(end) - np.array(start)            point_vec = np.array(point) - np.array(start)            line_len = np.linalg.norm(line_vec)            projection = np.dot(point_vec, line_vec) / line_len            projection = max(0, min(line_len, projection))            closest = np.array(start) + (projection / line_len) * line_vec            return np.linalg.norm(np.array(point) - closest)        def rdp(points, epsilon):            if len(points) < 3:                return points            dmax = 0            index = 0            for i in range(1, len(points) - 1):                d = point_line_distance(points[i], points[0], points[-1])                if d > dmax:                    index = i                    dmax = d            if dmax > epsilon:                left = rdp(points[:index + 1], epsilon)                right = rdp(points[index:], epsilon)                return left[:-1] + right            else:                return [points[0], points[-1]]        smoothed = rdp(path, tolerance)        # הוסף waypoints ביניים לחלקות        final = [smoothed[0]]        for i in range(len(smoothed) - 1):            # interpolate            dist = np.linalg.norm(np.array(smoothed[i+1]) - np.array(smoothed[i]))            n_points = max(1, int(dist / 20))  # נקודה כל 20 מטר            for j in range(1, n_points):                t = j / n_points                point = tuple(                    smoothed[i][k] + t * (smoothed[i+1][k] - smoothed[i][k])                    for k in range(3)                )                final.append(point)            final.append(smoothed[i+1])        return final66. טבלת מודולים סופית — גרסה 3.0#מודולתיאורקובץסטטוס1Coreפלטפורמה ליבהskycore/core/✅2Adaptersממשקי חומרהskycore/adapters/✅3Missionsתכנון SkyCore:67. מערכת סימולציית RF וקישוריות (RF Link Simulation)# skycore/rf/simulation.pyimport numpy as npfrom dataclasses import dataclassfrom typing import Dict, List, Optional, Tuplefrom enum import Enumimport logginglogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)class RFProtocol(Enum):    OCUSYNC = "ocusync"        # DJI proprietary    OCUSYNC_2 = "ocusync2"    OCUSYNC_3 = "ocusync3"    MAVLINK = "mavlink"        # open    WIFI = "wifi"              # 802.11    LTE = "lte"                # cellular    CUSTOM = "custom"@dataclassclass RFLinkBudget:    tx_power_dbm: float        # 20 for DJI    tx_gain_dbi: float         # antenna gain    rx_gain_dbi: float    rx_sensitivity_dbm: float   # -90 typical    frequency_ghz: float    bandwidth_mhz: float    modulation: str             # QPSK, 16QAM, etc.@dataclassclass RFEnvironment:    terrain_type: str          # urban, suburban, rural, water    vegetation_density: float    # 0-1    building_height_avg: float # meters    humidity_percent: float    rain_rate_mm_h: float      # 0 if clearclass RFLinkSimulator:    "סימולטור קישור RF"    # קבועים פיזיקליים    C = 299792458  # m/s    K_BOLTZMANN = 1.38e-23    T0 = 290  # K    def __init__(self, link_budget: RFLinkBudget, environment: RFEnvironment):        self.link = link_budget        self.env = environment        self._interference_sources: List[Dict] = []    def calculate_free_space_path_loss(        self,        distance_m: float,        frequency_ghz: float = None    ) -> float:        "חשב אבדן מרחב חופשי (FSPL)"        f = frequency_ghz or self.link.frequency_ghz        # FSPL = 20*log10(d) + 20*log10(f) + 20*log10(4π/c)        fspl = 20 * np.log10(distance_m) + 20 * np.log10(f * 1e9) + 20 * np.log10(4 * np.pi / self.C)        return fspl    def calculate_atmospheric_attenuation(self, distance_m: float) -> float:        "חשב אטנואציה אטמוספירית"        # תלות בתדירות ותנאים        f = self.link.frequency_ghz        # אדים        humidity_factor = 1 + (self.env.humidity_percent / 100) * 0.1        # גשם — ITU-R P.838        if self.env.rain_rate_mm_h > 0:            k = 0.036 * f ** 2.03  # approximate            alpha = 1.0            rain_attenuation = k * (self.env.rain_rate_mm_h ** alpha) * (distance_m / 1000)        else:            rain_attenuation = 0        # חמצן — חשוב מעל 10 GHz        if f > 10:            oxygen_attenuation = 0.007 * (distance_m / 1000) * (f / 20) ** 2        else:            oxygen_attenuation = 0        return (rain_attenuation + oxygen_attenuation) * humidity_factor    def calculate_multipath_fading(self, distance_m: float) -> float:        "חשב דעיכה מרובת מסלולים"        # Rayleigh/Rician model        # פשוט — log-normal shadowing        # תלות בסביבה        shadowing_std = {            'urban': 8,      # dB            'suburban': 6,            'rural': 4,            'water': 3        }.get(self.env.terrain_type, 6)        # תלות במרחק        if distance_m < 100:            # Rician — LOS probable            k_factor = 10  # strong LOS            fading = np.random.rayleigh(1) * 2  # dB scale        else:            # Rayleigh — NLOS likely            fading = np.random.rayleigh(2) * shadowing_std        return fading    def calculate_link_margin(        self,        distance_m: float,        altitude_tx_m: float = 0,        altitude_rx_m: float = 0    ) -> Dict:        "חשב מרווח קישור מלא"        # FSPL        fspl = self.calculate_free_space_path_loss(distance_m)        # atmospheric        atm = self.calculate_atmospheric_attenuation(distance_m)        # multipath        multipath = self.calculate_multipath_fading(distance_m)        # vegetation        veg_loss = self._vegetation_loss(distance_m)        # building penetration (if applicable)        bldg_loss = self._building_penetration(distance_m)        # total path loss        total_loss = fspl + atm + multipath + veg_loss + bldg_loss        # link budget        eirp = self.link.tx_power_dbm + self.link.tx_gain_dbi        rx_power = eirp - total_loss + self.link.rx_gain_dbi        # noise        noise_floor = self._calculate_noise_floor()        # SNR        snr = rx_power - noise_floor        # required SNR for modulation        required_snr = {            'BPSK': 6,            'QPSK': 10,            '16QAM': 16,            '64QAM': 22        }.get(self.link.modulation, 10)        margin = snr - required_snr        # throughput estimate        if margin > 10:            throughput_mbps = self.link.bandwidth_mhz * 4  # 16QAM equivalent        elif margin > 5:            throughput_mbps = self.link.bandwidth_mhz * 2  # QPSK        elif margin > 0:            throughput_mbps = self.link.bandwidth_mhz * 1  # BPSK        else:            throughput_mbps = 0        return {            'distance_m': distance_m,            'fspl_db': fspl,            'atmospheric_db': atm,            'multipath_db': multipath,            'vegetation_db': veg_loss,            'building_db': bldg_loss,            'total_loss_db': total_loss,            'rx_power_dbm': rx_power,            'noise_floor_dbm': noise_floor,            'snr_db': snr,            'required_snr_db': required_snr,            'link_margin_db': margin,            'throughput_mbps': throughput_mbps,            'link_status': 'strong' if margin > 10 else 'marginal' if margin > 0 else 'broken'        }    def _vegetation_loss(self, distance_m: float) -> float:        "אבדן צמחייה"        if self.env.vegetation_density < 0.1:            return 0        # Weissberger model (simplified)        if distance_m < 14:            loss = 0.45 * (self.env.vegetation_density ** 0.284) * (distance_m ** 0.588)        else:            loss = 1.33 * (self.env.vegetation_density ** 0.284) * (distance_m ** 0.588)        return loss * (1 + 0.5 * np.random.random())  # variability    def _building_penetration(self, distance_m: float) -> float:        "חדירת מבנים"        if self.env.terrain_type != 'urban':            return 0        # ITU-R P.2040        # probability of building obstruction increases with distance        obstruction_prob = min(1.0, distance_m / 500)        if np.random.random() < obstruction_prob:            # penetrate 1-2 walls            walls = np.random.randint(1, 3)            loss_per_wall = 10  # dB typical            return walls * loss_per_wall        return 0    def _calculate_noise_floor(self) -> float:        "רצפת רעש"        # thermal noise        noise_dbm = 10 * np.log10(self.K_BOLTZMANN * self.T0 * self.link.bandwidth_mhz * 1e6) + 30        # noise figure (typical 5 dB)        noise_figure = 5        # interference        interference = sum(            src['power_dbm'] - 10 * np.log10(1 + (src['frequency_ghz'] - self.link.frequency_ghz)**2 / 0.1)            for src in self._interference_sources        ) if self._interference_sources else 0        return noise_dbm + noise_figure + interference    def add_interference(self, source: Dict):        "הוסף מקור הפרעה"        self._interference_sources.append(source)    def simulate_flight_path(        self,        waypoints: List[Tuple[float, float, float]],        ground_station: Tuple[float, float, float]    ) -> List[Dict]:        "סימלץ קישור לאורך מסלול טיסה"        results = []        for i, wp in enumerate(waypoints):            # distance            dx = wp[0] - ground_station[0]            dy = wp[1] - ground_station[1]            dz = wp[2] - ground_station[2]            dist = np.sqrt(dx**2 + dy**2 + dz**2)            # altitude effects            link = self.calculate_link_margin(                dist,                altitude_tx_m=wp[2],                altitude_rx_m=ground_station[2]            )            results.append({                'waypoint': i,                'position': wp,                'distance_m': dist,                **link            })        return results    def recommend_antenna_orientation(        self,        drone_pos: Tuple[float, float, float],        ground_pos: Tuple[float, float, float]    ) -> Dict:        "המלך כיוון אנטנה"        dx = drone_pos[0] - ground_pos[0]        dy = drone_pos[1] - ground_pos[1]        dz = drone_pos[2] - ground_pos[2]        # azimuth        azimuth = np.degrees(np.arctan2(dy, dx))        if azimuth < 0:            azimuth += 360        # elevation        horizontal_dist = np.sqrt(dx**2 + dy**2)        elevation = np.degrees(np.arctan2(dz, horizontal_dist))        return {            'azimuth_deg': round(azimuth, 1),            'elevation_deg': round(elevation, 1),            'horizontal_distance_m': round(horizontal_dist, 1),            'recommendation': 'adjust' if abs(elevation) > 45 else 'optimal'        }    def calculate_frequency_hopping_pattern(        self,        base_frequency_ghz: float,        num_channels: int = 8,        bandwidth_mhz: float = 20    ) -> List[float]:        "חשב תבנית קפיצת תדר"        channels = []        for i in range(num_channels):            freq = base_frequency_ghz + (i - num_channels/2) * bandwidth_mhz / 1000            channels.append(freq)        # shuffle for hopping        np.random.shuffle(channels)        return channels68. מערכת ניהול מטען ומשקל (Payload & Weight Management)# skycore/payload/manager.pyfrom dataclasses import dataclassfrom typing import Dict, List, Optional, Tuplefrom enum import Enumimport logginglogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)class PayloadCategory(Enum):    CAMERA = "camera"    GIMBAL = "gimbal"    LIDAR = "lidar"    THERMAL = "thermal"    SPOTLIGHT = "spotlight"    SPEAKER = "speaker"    PARACHUTE = "parachute"    DELIVERY = "delivery"    SENSOR = "sensor"    ANTENNA = "antenna"@dataclassclass PayloadSpec:    payload_id: str    category: PayloadCategory    name: str    weight_g: float    dimensions_mm: Tuple[float, float, float]  # L, W, H    power_consumption_w: float    mounting_position: str  # top, bottom, front, side    cg_offset_mm: Tuple[float, float, float]  # offset from drone CG    aerodynamic_drag_coefficient: float    requires_gimbal: bool = False    requires_power: bool = True    requires_data: bool = True@dataclassclass CenterOfGravity:    x_mm: float    y_mm: float    z_mm: float    total_weight_g: float    moments: Dict[str, float]class PayloadManager:    "מנהל מטענים ומרכז כובד"    def __init__(self, drone_empty_weight_g: float, drone_cg_mm: Tuple[float, float, float]):        self.empty_weight = drone_empty_weight_g        self.empty_cg = drone_cg_mm        self.payloads: Dict[str, PayloadSpec] = {}        self._mounted: List[str] = []        self.max_takeoff_weight_g: float = 2000  # default    def add_payload(self, payload: PayloadSpec):        "הוסף מטען לקטלוג"        self.payloads[payload.payload_id] = payload        logger.info(f"מטען נוסף: {payload.name} ({payload.weight_g}g)")    def mount(self, payload_id: str) -> bool:        "הרכב מטען"        if payload_id not in self.payloads:            return False        # בדוק מגבלות        new_weight = self.calculate_total_weight() + self.payloads[payload_id].weight_g        if new_weight > self.max_takeoff_weight_g:            logger.warning("חריגה ממשקל המראה מקסימלי!")            return False        # בדוק התנגשות מיקום        position = self.payloads[payload_id].mounting_position        for mounted_id in self._mounted:            if self.payloads[mounted_id].mounting_position == position:                logger.warning(f"מיקום {position} תפוס על ידי {mounted_id}")                return False        self._mounted.append(payload_id)        logger.info(f"מטען {payload_id} הורכב")        return True    def unmount(self, payload_id: str):        "הסר מטען"        if payload_id in self._mounted:            self._mounted.remove(payload_id)    def calculate_total_weight(self) -> float:        "חשב משקל כולל"        payload_weight = sum(            self.payloads[p].weight_g for p in self._mounted        )        return self.empty_weight + payload_weight    def calculate_cg(self) -> CenterOfGravity:        "חשב מרכז כובד"        total_weight = self.empty_weight        # moments from empty drone        moment_x = self.empty_weight * self.empty_cg[0]        moment_y = self.empty_weight * self.empty_cg[1]        moment_z = self.empty_weight * self.empty_cg[2]        for payload_id in self._mounted:            p = self.payloads[payload_id]            total_weight += p.weight_g            moment_x += p.weight_g * (self.empty_cg[0] + p.cg_offset_mm[0])            moment_y += p.weight_g * (self.empty_cg[1] + p.cg_offset_mm[1])            moment_z += p.weight_g * (self.empty_cg[2] + p.cg_offset_mm[2])        cg = CenterOfGravity(            x_mm=moment_x / total_weight,            y_mm=moment_y / total_weight,            z_mm=moment_z / total_weight,            total_weight_g=total_weight,            moments={'x': moment_x, 'y': moment_y, 'z': moment_z}        )        return cg    def check_stability(self) -> Dict:        "בדוק יציבות"        cg = self.calculate_cg()        # distance from geometric center        offset = np.sqrt(            cg.x_mm**2 + cg.y_mm**2        )        # limits        max_offset_mm = 20  # typical for quadcopters        # power margin        hover_power = self._estimate_hover_power()        available_power = self._get_available_power()        return {            'cg_offset_mm': round(offset, 2),            'cg_offset_acceptable': offset < max_offset_mm,            'total_weight_g': cg.total_weight_g,            'weight_limit_g': self.max_takeoff_weight_g,            'weight_margin_g': self.max_takeoff_weight_g - cg.total_weight_g,            'hover_power_w': round(hover_power, 1),            'available_power_w': round(available_power, 1),            'power_margin_percent': round((available_power - hover_power) / available_power * 100, 1),            'stable': offset < max_offset_mm and hover_power < available_power * 0.8        }    def _estimate_hover_power(self) -> float:        "הערך הספק רחיפה"        weight_n = self.calculate_total_weight() / 1000 * 9.81        # figure of merit ~0.7        disk_area = 0.05  # m² per motor, 4 motors        power = weight_n ** 1.5 / np.sqrt(2 * 1.225 * disk_area) / 0.7        return power    def _get_available_power(self) -> float:        "הספק זמין"        # from battery and ESC limits        return 500  # W, typical    def calculate_flight_impact(self) -> Dict:        "חשב השפעה על ביצועי טיסה"        cg = self.calculate_cg()        weight = cg.total_weight_g        # endurance impact        base_endurance_min = 30  # empty        weight_factor = self.empty_weight / weight        estimated_endurance = base_endurance_min * weight_factor * 0.9  # 10% penalty for CG offset        # speed impact        base_speed_ms = 20        drag_increase = sum(            self.payloads[p].aerodynamic_drag_coefficient * 0.1            for p in self._mounted        )        estimated_speed = base_speed_ms * (1 - drag_increase)        # agility impact        base_agility = 1.0        inertia_increase = (weight / self.empty_weight) ** 2        estimated_agility = base_agility / inertia_increase        return {            'estimated_endurance_min': round(estimated_endurance, 1),            'estimated_max_speed_ms': round(estimated_speed, 1),            'estimated_agility': round(estimated_agility, 2),            'recommended_flight_mode': 'normal' if estimated_agility > 0.7 else 'cine' if estimated_agility > 0.4 else 'tripod'        }    def generate_mounting_diagram(self) -> Dict:        "צור תרשים הרכבה"        positions = {            'top': [],            'bottom': [],            'front': [],            'rear': [],            'left': [],            'right': []        }        for pid in self._mounted:            pos = self.payloads[pid].mounting_position            if pos in positions:                positions[pos].append({                    'id': pid,                    'name': self.payloads[pid].name,                    'weight_g': self.payloads[pid].weight_g                })        return {            'positions': positions,            'cg': {                'x': self.calculate_cg().x_mm,                'y': self.calculate_cg().y_mm            },            'warnings': [                f"משקל חריג: {self.calculate_total_weight()}g"                 if self.calculate_total_weight() > self.max_takeoff_weight_g * 0.9 else None            ]        }69. מערכת תיעוד וניהול סיכונים (Risk Management)# skycore/risk/management.pyfrom dataclasses import dataclassfrom datetime import datetimefrom typing import Dict, List, Optional, Tuplefrom enum import Enumimport numpy as npimport logginglogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)class RiskLevel(Enum):    NEGLIGIBLE = 1    LOW = 2    MEDIUM = 3    HIGH = 4    SEVERE = 5class RiskCategory(Enum):    OPERATIONAL = "operational"    TECHNICAL = "technical"    ENVIRONMENTAL = "environmental"    REGULATORY = "regulatory"    THIRD_PARTY = "third_party"    CYBER = "cyber"@dataclassclass RiskItem:    risk_id: str    category: RiskCategory    description: str    probability: float      # 0-1    severity: float         # 0-1 (impact)    existing_controls: List[str]    mitigation_measures: List[str]    residual_risk: float    # after mitigation    owner: str    review_date: datetimeclass RiskManagementSystem:    "מערכת ניהול סיכונים"    def __init__(self):        self.risks: Dict[str, RiskItem] = {}        self._risk_matrix = self._build_risk_matrix()        self._flight_history: List[Dict] = []    def _build_risk_matrix(self) -> np.ndarray:        "בנה מטריצת סיכונים"        # 5x5 matrix: probability x severity        matrix = np.array([            [1, 1, 2, 3, 4],   # very unlikely            [1, 2, 3, 4, 5],   # unlikely            [2, 3, 4, 5, 5],   # possible            [3, 4, 5, 5, 5],   # likely            [4, 5, 5, 5, 5]    # very likely        ])        return matrix    def register_risk(self, risk: RiskItem):        "רשום סיכון"        # חשב סיכון שיורי        inherent = risk.probability * risk.severity        mitigation_effectiveness = len(risk.mitigation_measures) * 0.15        residual = max(0, inherent - mitigation_effectiveness)        risk.residual_risk = residual        self.risks[risk.risk_id] = risk        logger.info(f"סיכון נרשם: {risk.risk_id} (רמת סיכון: {self._risk_to_level(residual).name})")    def _risk_to_level(self, risk_score: float) -> RiskLevel:        "המר ציון לרמה"        if risk_score < 0.05:            return RiskLevel.NEGLIGIBLE        elif risk_score < 0.15:            return RiskLevel.LOW        elif risk_score < 0.30:            return RiskLevel.MEDIUM        elif risk_score < 0.50:            return RiskLevel.HIGH        else:            return RiskLevel.SEVERE    def assess_flight(self, flight_plan: Dict) -> Dict:        "הערך סיכוני טיסה"        active_risks = []        # סיכוני מזג אוויר        weather = flight_plan.get('weather', {})        if weather.get('wind_speed_ms', 0) > 10:            active_risks.append({                'risk_id': 'ENV-001',                'description': 'רוח חזקה',                'probability': min(1.0, weather['wind_speed_ms'] / 20),                'severity': 0.4,                'mitigation': 'הפחת גובה, קצר טיסה'            })        if weather.get('precipitation_probability', 0) > 0.3:            active_risks.append({                'risk_id': 'ENV-002',                'description': 'משקעים',                'probability': weather['precipitation_probability'],                'severity': 0.3,                'mitigation': 'דחה טיסה או השתמש במגן מים'            })        # סיכוני מרחב אווירי        if flight_plan.get('airspace_class') in ['B', 'C', 'D']:            active_risks.append({                'risk_id': 'REG-001',                'description': 'מרחב אווירי מבוקר',                'probability': 0.3,                'severity': 0.7,                'mitigation': 'קבל אישור ATC'            })        # סיכוני טכניים        battery = flight_plan.get('battery', {})        if battery.get('state_of_health', 100) < 80:            active_risks.append({                'risk_id': 'TEC-001',                'description': 'סוללה מזדקנת',                'probability': 0.2,                'severity': 0.6,                'mitigation': 'החלף סוללה'            })        # סיכון אנושי        if flight_plan.get('over_people', False):            active_risks.append({                'risk_id': 'OPS-001',                'description': 'טיסה מעל אנשים',                'probability': 0.1,                'severity': 0.9,                'mitigation': 'השתמש ב-parachute, הגבל גובה'            })        # חשב סיכון כולל        total_risk = 1 - np.prod([            1 - (r['probability'] * r['severity'])             for r in active_risks        ])        # המלצות        if total_risk > 0.5:            recommendation = 'abort'        elif total_risk > 0.3:            recommendation = 'mitigate_before_flight'        elif total_risk > 0.15:            recommendation = 'proceed_with_caution'        else:            recommendation = 'proceed'        return {            'total_risk_score': round(total_risk, 3),            'risk_level': self._risk_to_level(total_risk).name,            'active_risks': active_risks,            'recommendation': recommendation,            'required_mitigations': [                r['mitigation'] for r in active_risks                 if r['probability'] * r['severity'] > 0.1            ],            'requires_supervisor_approval': total_risk > 0.3        }    def record_flight_outcome(self, flight_id: str, plan: Dict, outcome: Dict):        "רשום תוצאת טיסה ללמידה"        self._flight_history.append({            'flight_id': flight_id,            'planned_risks': self.assess_flight(plan),            'actual_issues': outcome.get('issues', []),            'incidents': outcome.get('incidents', []),            'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat()        })        # עדכן הסתברויות מבוסס נתונים        self._update_probabilities()    def _update_probabilities(self):        "עדכן הסתברויות מנתוני עבר"        for risk in self.risks.values():            # מצא טיסות דומות            relevant = [                f for f in self._flight_history                if any(r['risk_id'] == risk.risk_id for r in f['planned_risks'].get('active_risks', []))            ]            if len(relevant) > 10:                # חשב שכיחות בפועל                occurred = sum(1 for f in relevant if any(                    i.get('related_risk') == risk.risk_id                     for i in f['actual_issues']                ))                # עדכן עם Bayesian smoothing                new_prob = (occurred + 1) / (len(relevant) + 2)                risk.probability = 0.7 * risk.probability + 0.3 * new_prob    def generate_risk_register(self) -> str:        "צור רישום סיכונים"        lines = [            "# Risk Register",            "",            "| ID | Category | Description | Probability | Severity | Residual | Level |",            "|----|----------|-------------|-------------|----------|----------|-------|"        ]        for risk in self.risks.values():            level = self._risk_to_level(risk.residual_risk)            lines.append(                f"| {risk.risk_id} | {risk.category.value} | {risk.description} | "                f"{risk.probability:.2f} | {risk.severity:.2f} | "                f"{risk.residual_risk:.2f} | {level.name} |"            )        return "\n".join(lines)    def get_insurance_recommendation(self) -> Dict:        "המלצות ביטוח"        high_risks = [            r for r in self.risks.values()             if self._risk_to_level(r.residual_risk) in [RiskLevel.HIGH, RiskLevel.SEVERE]        ]        coverage_needed = sum(            r.severity * 100000 for r in high_risks  # $100k per severity unit        )        return {            'recommended_coverage_usd': round(coverage_needed, -3),            'third_party_liability': max(1000000, round(coverage_needed * 2, -3)),            'hull_coverage': 15000,  # typical drone value            'payload_coverage': 5000,            'premium_estimate_annual': round(coverage_needed * 0.02, -2),  # 2% of coverage            'risk_mitigation_discount': len(high_risks) < 3  # discount if few high risks        }70. טבלת מודולים סופית — גרסה 4.0#מודולתיאורקובץסטטוס1Coreפלטפורמה ליבהskycore/core/✅2Adaptersממשקי
