מכונה מתקדמת (Advanced ML)# skycore/ml/advanced.pyimport numpy as npfrom sklearn.ensemble import IsolationForest, RandomForestRegressorfrom sklearn.cluster import DBSCANfrom sklearn.preprocessing import StandardScalerimport tensorflow as tffrom typing import Dict, List, Optional, Tupleimport logginglogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)class AnomalyDetectionEngine:    "מנוע זיהוי אנומליות מתקדם"    def __init__(self):        self.models = {            'telemetry': IsolationForest(contamination=0.1, random_state=42),            'battery': IsolationForest(contamination=0.05, random_state=42),            'motor': IsolationForest(contamination=0.05, random_state=42),            'gps': IsolationForest(contamination=0.02, random_state=42)        }        self.scalers = {name: StandardScaler() for name in self.models}        self._trained = False        self._history_buffer = {name: [] for name in self.models}    def train(self, historical_data: Dict[str, np.ndarray]):        "אמן מודלים על נתוני עבר"        for name, data in historical_data.items():            if name in self.models and len(data) > 100:                scaled = self.scalers[name].fit_transform(data)                self.models[name].fit(scaled)                logger.info(f"מודל {name} אומן על {len(data)} דגימות")        self._trained = True    def detect(self, telemetry_snapshot: Dict) -> Dict[str, List[dict]]:        "זהה אנומליות בזמן אמת"        if not self._trained:            return {}        anomalies = {}        # Telemetry anomalies        if 'imu' in telemetry_snapshot:            imu_features = self._extract_imu_features(telemetry_snapshot['imu'])            scaled = self.scalers['telemetry'].transform([imu_features])            prediction = self.models['telemetry'].predict(scaled)[0]            if prediction == -1:  # anomaly                anomalies['telemetry'] = [{                    'type': 'imu_anomaly',                    'confidence': 0.85,                    'features': imu_features.tolist(),                    'recommendation': 'check_vibrations'                }]        # Battery anomalies        if 'battery' in telemetry_snapshot:            batt_features = self._extract_battery_features(telemetry_snapshot['battery'])            scaled = self.scalers['battery'].transform([batt_features])            prediction = self.models['battery'].predict(scaled)[0]            if prediction == -1:                anomalies['battery'] = [{                    'type': 'battery_degradation',                    'confidence': 0.90,                    'features': batt_features.tolist(),                    'recommendation': 'replace_battery'                }]        # GPS anomalies (spoofing/jamming detection)        if 'gps' in telemetry_snapshot:            gps_features = self._extract_gps_features(telemetry_snapshot['gps'])            scaled = self.scalers['gps'].transform([gps_features])            prediction = self.models['gps'].predict(scaled)[0]            if prediction == -1:                anomalies['gps'] = [{                    'type': 'gps_spoofing_detected',                    'confidence': 0.95,                    'features': gps_features.tolist(),                    'recommendation': 'switch_to_ins'                }]        return anomalies    def _extract_imu_features(self, imu_data: dict) -> np.ndarray:        "חלץ תכונות IMU"        return np.array([            np.linalg.norm(imu_data.get('accel', [0,0,0])),            np.linalg.norm(imu_data.get('gyro', [0,0,0])),            np.std(imu_data.get('accel_history', [0])),            np.std(imu_data.get('gyro_history', [0]))        ])    def _extract_battery_features(self, battery_data: dict) -> np.ndarray:        "חלץ תכונות סוללה"        return np.array([            battery_data.get('voltage', 0),            battery_data.get('current', 0),            battery_data.get('temperature', 0),            battery_data.get('cycle_count', 0),            battery_data.get('internal_resistance', 0)        ])    def _extract_gps_features(self, gps_data: dict) -> np.ndarray:        "חלץ תכונות GPS"        return np.array([            gps_data.get('hdop', 99),            gps_data.get('satellites', 0),            gps_data.get('speed_accuracy', 999),            gps_data.get('position_accuracy', 999)        ])class PredictiveFailureModel:    "מודל חיזוי כשלים"    def __init__(self):        self.failure_predictor = RandomForestRegressor(            n_estimators=200,            max_depth=10,            random_state=42        )        self._trained = False    def train(self, features: np.ndarray, time_to_failure: np.ndarray):        "אמן על נתוני כשל היסטוריים"        self.failure_predictor.fit(features, time_to_failure)        self._trained = True        logger.info("מודל חיזוי כשלים אומן")    def predict_time_to_failure(self, current_features: np.ndarray) -> Dict:        "חזה זמן לכשל"        if not self._trained:            return {'error': 'not_trained'}        prediction = self.failure_predictor.predict([current_features])[0]        confidence = self.failure_predictor.score(            [current_features],             [prediction]        )        return {            'estimated_hours_remaining': float(prediction),            'confidence': float(confidence),            'urgency': 'critical' if prediction < 10 else 'high' if prediction < 50 else 'medium'        }class NeuralTrajectoryPlanner:    "מתכנן מסלול מבוסס רשת נוירונים"    def __init__(self, model_path: Optional[str] = None):        if model_path:            self.model = tf.keras.models.load_model(model_path)        else:            self.model = self._build_model()    def _build_model(self) -> tf.keras.Model:        "בנה רשת נוירונים"        model = tf.keras.Sequential([            tf.keras.layers.LSTM(128, return_sequences=True, input_shape=(100, 6)),            tf.keras.layers.LSTM(64),            tf.keras.layers.Dense(128, activation='relu'),            tf.keras.layers.Dense(64, activation='relu'),            tf.keras.layers.Dense(3)  # x, y, z output        ])        model.compile(            optimizer='adam',            loss='mse',            metrics=['mae']        )        return model    def predict_optimal_path(        self,        start: Tuple[float, float, float],        goal: Tuple[float, float, float],        obstacles: List[Tuple[float, float, float, float]],  # x, y, z, radius        wind_vector: Tuple[float, float, float]    ) -> List[Tuple[float, float, float]]:        "חזה מסלול אופטימלי"        # הכן input sequence        sequence = self._prepare_sequence(start, goal, obstacles, wind_vector)        # predict        predictions = []        current = np.array(start)        for _ in range(100):  # max 100 waypoints            pred = self.model.predict([sequence])[0]            current = current + pred            predictions.append(tuple(current))            if np.linalg.norm(current - np.array(goal)) < 5:                break            # update sequence            sequence = self._update_sequence(sequence, current)        return predictions    def _prepare_sequence(        self,        start: Tuple[float, float, float],        goal: Tuple[float, float, float],        obstacles: List,        wind: Tuple[float, float, float]    ) -> np.ndarray:        "הכן רצף קלט"        sequence = []        for _ in range(100):            features = [                start[0], start[1], start[2],                goal[0], goal[1], goal[2],                wind[0], wind[1], wind[2],                len(obstacles)            ]            sequence.append(features[:6])  # take first 6        return np.array([sequence])    def _update_sequence(self, sequence: np.ndarray, new_position: np.ndarray) -> np.ndarray:        "עדכן רצף עם מיקום חדש"        # roll and update        new_seq = np.roll(sequence, -1, axis=1)        new_seq[0, -1, :3] = new_position        return new_seq46. מערכת עיבוד שפה טבעית (NLP) לפקודות קוליות# skycore/voice/nlp.pyimport refrom typing import Dict, List, Optional, Tuplefrom dataclasses import dataclassfrom enum import Enumimport logginglogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)class IntentType(Enum):    TAKEOFF = "takeoff"    LAND = "land"    GOTO = "goto"    RTL = "return_to_launch"    ORBIT = "orbit"    FOLLOW = "follow"    RECORD = "record"    PHOTO = "photo"    EMERGENCY = "emergency"    STATUS = "status"    CANCEL = "cancel"@dataclassclass ParsedCommand:    intent: IntentType    confidence: float    parameters: Dict    original_text: str    language: strclass VoiceCommandParser:    "פארסר פקודות קוליות"    def __init__(self, supported_languages: List[str] = None):        self.languages = supported_languages or ['en', 'he', 'ar']        self._patterns = self._compile_patterns()    def _compile_patterns(self) -> Dict[str, Dict[IntentType, List[str]]]:        "הדר גלובליים לכל שפה"        return {            'en': {                IntentType.TAKEOFF: [                    r'take\s*off',                    r'launch',                    r'fly',                    r'up'                ],                IntentType.LAND: [                    r'land',                    r'come\s*down',                    r'set\s*down'                ],                IntentType.RTL: [                    r'return\s*home',                    r'come\s*back',                    r'rtl'                ],                IntentType.EMERGENCY: [                    r'stop',                    r'hold',                    r'emergency',                    r'abort'                ]            },            'he': {                IntentType.TAKEOFF: [                    r'המריא',                    r'התרומם',                    r'טוס'                ],                IntentType.LAND: [                    r'נחת',                    r'הורד',                    r'למטה'                ],                IntentType.RTL: [                    r'חזור',                    r'הביתה',                    r'בחזרה'                ],                IntentType.EMERGENCY: [                    r'עצור',                    r'חירום',                    r'הפסק'                ]            }        }    def parse(self, text: str, language: str = 'en') -> ParsedCommand:        "פארס טקסט לפקודה"        text_lower = text.lower().strip()        # זהה שפה אם לא סופקה        if language == 'auto':            language = self._detect_language(text_lower)        patterns = self._patterns.get(language, self._patterns['en'])        best_match = None        best_confidence = 0        for intent, regex_list in patterns.items():            for pattern in regex_list:                if re.search(pattern, text_lower):                    confidence = len(pattern) / len(text_lower)  # simple heuristic                    if confidence > best_confidence:                        best_confidence = confidence                        best_match = intent        if best_match:            params = self._extract_parameters(text_lower, best_match)            return ParsedCommand(                intent=best_match,                confidence=min(1.0, best_confidence * 2),                parameters=params,                original_text=text,                language=language            )        # לא זוהה — נסה fuzzy matching        return self._fuzzy_match(text_lower, language)    def _detect_language(self, text: str) -> str:        "זהה שפה מהטקסט"        # פשוט — בדוק תווים        if any('\u0590' <= c <= '\u05FF' for c in text):            return 'he'        if any('\u0600' <= c <= '\u06FF' for c in text):            return 'ar'        return 'en'    def _extract_parameters(self, text: str, intent: IntentType) -> Dict:        "חלץ פרמטרים מהטקסט"        params = {}        if intent == IntentType.GOTO:            # חפש קואורדינטות או מיקומים            coord_pattern = r'(\d+\.?\d*)\s*[°,]\s*(\d+\.?\d*)'            match = re.search(coord_pattern, text)            if match:                params['latitude'] = float(match.group(1))                params['longitude'] = float(match.group(2))            # גובה            alt_pattern = r'(\d+)\s*(meters?|m|feet|ft)'            alt_match = re.search(alt_pattern, text)            if alt_match:                params['altitude'] = float(alt_match.group(1))                if 'ft' in alt_match.group(2):                    params['altitude'] *= 0.3048        elif intent == IntentType.ORBIT:            # רדיוס            radius_pattern = r'(\d+)\s*(meters?|m)'            match = re.search(radius_pattern, text)            if match:                params['radius_m'] = float(match.group(1))        elif intent == IntentType.FOLLOW:            # מטרה            targets = ['person', 'car', 'me', 'target']            for target in targets:                if target in text:                    params['target'] = target        return params    def _fuzzy_match(self, text: str, language: str) -> ParsedCommand:        "התאמה מטושטשת"        # Levenshtein distance פשוט        all_patterns = []        for intent, patterns in self._patterns.get(language, {}).items():            for p in patterns:                all_patterns.append((intent, p))        best_score = float('inf')        best_intent = None        for intent, pattern in all_patterns:            score = self._levenshtein(text, pattern)            if score < best_score:                best_score = score                best_intent = intent        if best_score < len(text) * 0.3:  # threshold            return ParsedCommand(                intent=best_intent,                confidence=max(0, 1 - best_score / len(text)),                parameters={},                original_text=text,                language=language            )        return ParsedCommand(            intent=IntentType.STATUS,            confidence=0.1,            parameters={},            original_text=text,            language=language        )    def _levenshtein(self, s1: str, s2: str) -> int:        "חשב מרחק Levenshtein"        if len(s1) < len(s2):            return self._levenshtein(s2, s1)        if len(s2) == 0:            return len(s1)        previous_row = range(len(s2) + 1)        for i, c1 in enumerate(s1):            current_row = [i + 1]            for j, c2 in enumerate(s2):                insertions = previous_row[j + 1] + 1                deletions = current_row[j] + 1                substitutions = previous_row[j] + (c1 != c2)                current_row.append(min(insertions, deletions, substitutions))            previous_row = current_row        return previous_row[-1]    def generate_confirmation(self, command: ParsedCommand) -> str:        "צור הודעת אישור"        confirmations = {            'en': {                IntentType.TAKEOFF: "Taking off now",                IntentType.LAND: "Landing initiated",                IntentType.RTL: "Returning to launch point",                IntentType.EMERGENCY: "Emergency stop activated",                IntentType.GOTO: f"Going to {command.parameters.get('latitude', '?')}, {command.parameters.get('longitude', '?')}",                IntentType.ORBIT: f"Orbiting with radius {command.parameters.get('radius_m', '?')} meters"            },            'he': {                IntentType.TAKEOFF: "ממריא עכשיו",                IntentType.LAND: "מתחיל נחיתה",                IntentType.RTL: "חוזר לנקודת המראה",                IntentType.EMERGENCY: "עצירת חירום הופעלה",                IntentType.GOTO: f"טס ל-{command.parameters.get('latitude', '?')}, {command.parameters.get('longitude', '?')}",                IntentType.ORBIT: f"מקיף ברדיוס {command.parameters.get('radius_m', '?')} מטר"            }        }        return confirmations.get(command.language, confirmations['en']).get(            command.intent,             "Command confirmed"        )47. מערכת אינטגרציה עם רכבים מאוישים (Manned Aircraft Integration)# skycore/adsb/integration.pyimport asynciofrom dataclasses import dataclassfrom datetime import datetime, timedeltafrom typing import Dict, List, Optional, Tupleimport logginglogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)@dataclassclass ADSBMessage:    icao_address: str    callsign: Optional[str]    position: Tuple[float, float, float]  # lat, lon, alt    velocity: Tuple[float, float, float]   # vx, vy, vz    heading: float    vertical_rate: float    squawk: Optional[str]    emergency_status: bool    timestamp: datetimeclass ADSBReceiver:    "מקלט ADS-B"    def __init__(self, source: str = "dump1090"):        self.source = source        self._aircraft: Dict[str, ADSBMessage] = {}        self._callbacks: List[Callable] = []        self._running = False    async def start(self):        "התחל קבלה"        self._running = True        if self.source == "dump1090":            await self._connect_dump1090()        elif self.source == "opensky":            await self._connect_opensky()        elif self.source == "simulation":            await self._run_simulation()    async def _connect_dump1090(self):        "חבר ל-dump1090 (RTL-SDR)"        # Beast format over TCP        reader, writer = await asyncio.open_connection('localhost', 30005)        while self._running:            try:                # Beast frame: <0x1a> <type> <data...>                data = await reader.read(1)                if data == b'\x1a':                    frame_type = await reader.read(1)                    frame_data = await reader.read(7 if frame_type == b'\x33' else 14)                    msg = self._parse_beast_frame(frame_type, frame_data)                    if msg:                        self._update_aircraft(msg)            except asyncio.CancelledError:                break            except Exception as e:                logger.error(f"ADS-B error: {e}")                await asyncio.sleep(1)    def _parse_beast_frame(self, frame_type: bytes, data: bytes) -> Optional[ADSBMessage]:        "פארס פריים Beast"        # Mode S Extended Squitter        if len(data) < 11:            return None        # ICAO address        icao = data[0:3].hex().upper()        # Position (simplified — needs proper decoding)        # TODO: full CPR algorithm        return ADSBMessage(            icao_address=icao,            callsign=None,            position=(0, 0, 0),            velocity=(0, 0, 0),            heading=0,            vertical_rate=0,            squawk=None,            emergency_status=False,            timestamp=datetime.now()        )    def _update_aircraft(self, msg: ADSBMessage):        "עדכן מטוס במאגר"        self._aircraft[msg.icao_address] = msg        # בדוק התנגשות        self._check_proximity(msg)        # קרא callbacks        for cb in self._callbacks:            asyncio.create_task(cb(msg))    def _check_proximity(self, msg: ADSBMessage):        "בדוק קרבה לרחפן"        # TODO: קבל מיקום רחפן        drone_position = (32.0853, 34.7818, 100)  # placeholder        distance = self._haversine(            msg.position[0], msg.position[1],            drone_position[0], drone_position[1]        )        altitude_diff = abs(msg.position[2] - drone_position[2])        if distance < 1000 and altitude_diff < 300:  # 1km, 300m            logger.warning(                f"מטוס קרוב! {msg.callsign or msg.icao_address} "                f"במרחק {distance:.0f}מ', הפרש גובה {altitude_diff:.0f}מ'"            )    def _haversine(self, lat1, lon1, lat2, lon2) -> float:        "מרחק גיאודטי"        R = 6371000        phi1, phi2 = np.radians(lat1), np.radians(lat2)        dphi = np.radians(lat2 - lat1)        dlambda = np.radians(lon2 - lon1)        a = np.sin(dphi/2)**2 + np.cos(phi1)*np.cos(phi2)*np.sin(dlambda/2)**2        return 2 * R * np.arcsin(np.sqrt(a))    def get_nearby_aircraft(        self,        position: Tuple[float, float, float],        radius_m: float = 5000,        max_altitude_diff_m: float = 500    ) -> List[ADSBMessage]:        "קבל מטוסים בקרבה"        nearby = []        for aircraft in self._aircraft.values():            # בדוק תפוגה            if datetime.now() - aircraft.timestamp > timedelta(seconds=30):                continue            distance = self._haversine(                position[0], position[1],                aircraft.position[0], aircraft.position[1]            )            alt_diff = abs(position[2] - aircraft.position[2])            if distance < radius_m and alt_diff < max_altitude_diff_m:                nearby.append(aircraft)        return sorted(nearby, key=lambda a: self._haversine(            position[0], position[1],            a.position[0], a.position[1]        ))    def on_aircraft_detected(self, callback: Callable):        "רשם callback למטוס חדש"        self._callbacks.append(callback)    async def _connect_opensky(self):        "חבר ל-OpenSky Network API"        while self._running:            try:                async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as session:                    # Bounding box query                    url = "https://opensky-network.org/api/states/all"                    params = {                        'lamin': 29.5, 'lamax': 33.5,                        'lomin': 34.0, 'lomax': 35.5                    }                    async with session.get(url, params=params) as response:                        data = await response.json()                        for state in data.get('states', []):                            msg = self._state_to_message(state)                            if msg:                                self._update_aircraft(msg)            except Exception as e:                logger.error(f"OpenSky error: {e}")            await asyncio.sleep(10)  # poll every 10 seconds    def _state_to_message(self, state: List) -> Optional[ADSBMessage]:        "המר state OpenSky ל-ADSBMessage"        if not state or len(state) < 17:            return None        return ADSBMessage(            icao_address=state[0],            callsign=state[1].strip() if state[1] else None,            position=(state[6], state[5], state[7] * 0.3048) if state[6] else (0, 0, 0),            velocity=(state[9], 0, 0) if state[9] else (0, 0, 0),            heading=state[10] or 0,            vertical_rate=state[11] or 0,            squawk=state[14],            emergency_status=state[15] or False,            timestamp=datetime.fromtimestamp(state[4] or 0)        )    async def _run_simulation(self):        "הרץ סימולציית מטוסים"        # יציר מטוסים וירטואליים לבדיקה        simulated_aircraft = [            {                'icao': 'SIM001',                'route': [(32.0, 34.5, 3000), (32.1, 34.6, 3000)],                'speed': 100  # m/s            }        ]        while self._running:            for ac in simulated_aircraft:                # התקדם לאורך המסלול                # TODO: interpolation                msg = ADSBMessage(                    icao_address=ac['icao'],                    callsign='SIM1',                    position=ac['route'][0],                    velocity=(ac['speed'], 0, 0),                    heading=45,                    vertical_rate=0,                    squawk='1200',                    emergency_status=False,                    timestamp=datetime.now()                )                self._update_aircraft(msg)            await asyncio.sleep(1)48. טבלת מודולים סופית — גרסה
